Topic: Barbie ### Response:  Question: Barbie has 500 pairs of shoes. 200 are high heels, 150 are flats, and the rest are sneakers. How many pairs of sneakers does Barbie have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Barbie has 500 pairs of shoes
    shoes_total = 500
    #200 are high heels
    high_heels = 200
    #150 are flats
    flats = 150
    #The rest are sneakers. The answer is
    sneakers = shoes_total - high_heels - flats
    return sneakers
Topic: Black Panther ### Response:  Question: Black Panther can run 200 meters in 20 seconds. How long does it take him to run 100 meters?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Black Panther can run 200 meters in 20 seconds
    time_200 = 20
    #100 meters is half of 200 meters
    meters_100 = 200 / 2
    #The answer is
    result = time_200 / meters_100
    return result

Topic: cookies ### Response: 
Question: 
A cookie baker has 2500 cookies. 
He sells 1000 cookies in the morning, 
200 cookies in the afternoon, 
and 500 cookies in the evening. 
How many cookies does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The baker started with 2500 cookies
    cookies_initial = 2500
    #He sold 1000 cookies in the morning
    cookies_sold_morning = 1000
    #200 cookies in the afternoon
    cookies_sold_afternoon = 200
    #And 500 cookies in the evening
    cookies_sold_evening = 500
    #The answer is
    result = cookies_initial - cookies_sold_morning - cookies_sold_afternoon - cookies_sold_evening
    return result
Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Iron Man has a total of 42 suits. 25 of the suits are gold. 10 of the suits are red. 7 of the suits are blue. How many of the suits are not blue?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man has a total of 42 suits
    suits_total = 42
    #25 of the suits are gold
    gold_suits = 25
    #10 of the suits are red
    red_suits = 10
    #7 of the suits are blue
    blue_suits = 7
    #The answer is
    result = suits_total - gold_suits - red_suits - blue_suits
    return result
Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizza has 8 slices. 2 of the slices have mushrooms. 5 of the slices have pepperoni. 1 of the slices has both mushrooms and pepperoni. How many slices do not have either topping?

Solution:
def solution():
    #A pizza has 8 slices
    pizza_slices = 8
    #2 slices have mushrooms
    slices_mushrooms = 2
    #5 slices have pepperoni
    slices_pepperoni = 5
    #1 slice has both mushrooms and pepperoni
    slices_both = 1
    #The answer is
    result = pizza_slices - slices_mushrooms - slices_pepperoni + slices_both
    return result
Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizza has 8 slices. If 2 slices are pepperoni, 3 slices are cheese, and 1 slice is vegetarian, how many slices have neither pepperoni nor cheese?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total slices
    total_slices = 8
    #Pepperoni slices
    pepperoni_slices = 2
    #Cheese slices
    cheese_slices = 3
    #Vegetarian slices
    vegetarian_slices = 1
    #Slices with neither pepperoni nor cheese
    neither_pepperoni_nor_cheese_slices = total_slices - pepperoni_slices - cheese_slices + vegetarian_slices
    return neither_pepperoni_nor_cheese_slices
Topic: Harry Potter ### Response: 
Question: In the Harry Potter books, a witch or wizard can cast a spell by saying a magical phrase. Hermione, a witch, has a spell-book with 200 pages. Each page has 2 spells. She can cast 3 spells per day. How many days will it take for her to cast all the spells in the book?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Hermione has a spell-book with 200 pages
    pages_in_book = 200
    #Each page has 2 spells
    spells_per_page = 2
    #She can cast 3 spells per day
    spells_per_day = 3
    #The answer is
    result = (pages_in_book * spells_per_page) / spells_per_day
    return result

Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can fly at 3,000 mph
    superman_speed = 3000
    #He is 10,000 miles away from the sun
    distance = 10000
    #The answer is
    result = distance / superman_speed
    return result

Topic: Superman ### Response: 
Question: Superman can fly 1000 miles in 2 hours. How many miles can he fly in 5 hours?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can fly 1000 miles in 2 hours
    miles_2_hours = 1000
    #5 hours is 300 minutes
    minutes_5_hours = 300
    #The answer is
    result = (miles_2_hours / 2) * minutes_5_hours
    return result

Topic: Superman ### Response:  Question: Superman can fly at a speed of 1000 miles per hour. A one-way trip from Metropolis to Gotham City is 300 miles. How long does it take him to make a round trip?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can fly at a speed of 1000 miles per hour
    superman_speed = 1000
    #A one-way trip from Metropolis to Gotham City is 300 miles
    one_way_trip = 300
    #A round trip is two one-way trips
    round_trip = 2 * one_way_trip
    #The answer is
    result = round_trip / superman_speed
    return result
Topic: soccer ### Response: 
Question: 1200 people are at a soccer match. 1000 of them are wearing the home team's jersey. 150 of the away team's fans are wearing the away team's jersey. 50 of the people at the match are wearing a jersey of a different soccer team. How many people at the match are not wearing any soccer jerseys?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total people at the match
    total_people = 1200
    #Home team fans
    home_team_fans = 1000
    #Away team fans
    away_team_fans = 150
    #Other team fans
    other_team_fans = 50
    #Fans wearing no jersey
    no_jersey_fans = total_people - home_team_fans - away_team_fans - other_team_fans
    return no_jersey_fans

    total_soldiers = 3000
    #Soldiers in the field
    soldiers_field = 1000
    #Soldiers in the lab
    soldiers_lab = 500
    #Soldiers in the training room are

    return soldiers_training

Topic: Pokémon ### Response: 
Question: Ash has 50 Pokémon. Brock has 30 more Pokémon than Ash. Misty has 20 fewer Pokémon than Brock. How many Pokémon do the three have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Ash has 50 Pokémon
    ash_pokemon = 50
    #Brock has 30 more Pokémon than Ash
    brock_pokemon = ash_pokemon + 30
    #Misty has 20 fewer Pokémon than Brock
    misty_pokemon = brock_pokemon - 20
    #The total number of Pokémon is
    total_pokemon = ash_pokemon + brock_pokemon + misty_pokemon
    return total_pokemon

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: A dinosaur is 30 feet long. He is 15 feet tall. How many feet is he from head to tail?

Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Iron Man has 100 suits. He uses 10 suits per mission. How many suits does he have left after 5 missions?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man started with 100 suits
    suits_initial = 100
    #He uses 10 suits per mission
    suits_per_mission = 10
    #There are 5 missions
    num_missions = 5
    #Suits used is
    suits_used = suits_per_mission * num_missions
    #The answer is
    result = suits_initial - suits_used
    return result

Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena Williams has won 23 Grand Slam singles titles.  She has won 14 in doubles and 2 in mixed doubles.  How many Grand Slam titles has Serena Williams won in total?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams has won 23 Grand Slam singles titles
    singles = 23
    #She has won 14 in doubles
    doubles = 14
    #She has won 2 in mixed doubles
    mixed_doubles = 2
    #The answer is
    result = singles + doubles + mixed_doubles
    return result
Topic: soccer ### Response: 
Question: The soccer team has 22 players. 11 of them are on the field, and the rest are on the bench. 5 of the players on the bench are goalies. 2 of the goalies are left-handed. How many right-handed goalies are on the bench?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The soccer team has 22 players
    total_players = 22
    #11 of them are on the field
    players_on_field = 11
    #The rest are on the bench
    players_on_bench = total_players - players_on_field
    #5 of the players on the bench are goalies
    goalies_on_bench = 5
    #2 of the goalies are left-handed
    left_handed_goalies = 2
    #The answer is
    right_handed_goalies = goalies_on_bench - left_handed_goalies
    return right_handed_goalies

Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response: 
Question: Thor has 200 lightning bolts. 20 of them are in Asgard, 50 of them are in Jotunheim, and the rest are in Midgard. How many lightning bolts does Thor have in Midgard?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Thor has 200 lightning bolts
    lightning_bolts = 200
    #20 of them are in Asgard
    asgard_bolts = 20
    #50 of them are in Jotunheim
    jotunheim_bolts = 50
    #The rest are in Midgard
    midgard_bolts = lightning_bolts - asgard_bolts - jotunheim_bolts
    #The answer is

    return result
Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: The ice cream truck has 24 cones. 1/3 of them are chocolate. 1/2 of them are vanilla. 1/6 of them are strawberry. How many of the cones are not chocolate, vanilla, or strawberry?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The ice cream truck has 24 cones
    cones = 24
    #1/3 of them are chocolate
    chocolate_cones = cones * 1/3
    #1/2 of them are vanilla
    vanilla_cones = cones * 1/2
    #1/6 of them are strawberry
    strawberry_cones = cones * 1/6
    #The answer is
    result = cones - (chocolate_cones + vanilla_cones + strawberry_cones)
    return result

Topic: Batman ### Response: 
Question: Batman has 200 Batarangs. 100 of the Batarangs are blue, and the rest are red. 50 of the red Batarangs are in his Batmobile, and the rest are in his Batcave. How many red Batarangs are in his Batcave?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Batman has 200 Batarangs
    batarangs = 200
    #100 of the Batarangs are blue
    blue_batarangs = 100
    #The rest are red
    red_batarangs = batarangs - blue_batarangs
    #50 of the red Batarangs are in his Batmobile
    red_batarangs_in_batmobile = 50
    #The rest are in his Batcave
    red_batarangs_in_batcave = red_batarangs - red_batarangs_in_batmobile
    #The answer is
    result = red_batarangs_in_batcave
    return result

Topic: Black Panther ### Response: 
Question: Wakanda has 1000 war rhinos. 100 of them are black. 200 are white. 300 are brown. 400 are grey. How many are not one of these colors?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of war rhinos
    total_war_rhinos = 1000
    #Number of black war rhinos
    black_war_rhinos = 100
    #Number of white war rhinos
    white_war_rhinos = 200
    #Number of brown war rhinos
    brown_war_rhinos = 300
    #Number of grey war rhinos
    grey_war_rhinos = 400
    #The answer is
    result = total_war_rhinos - black_war_rhinos - white_war_rhinos - brown_war_rhinos - grey_war_rhinos
    return result
Topic: basketball ### Response: 
Question: In the 1998 NBA Finals, Michael Jordan scored 38.5 points per game. He scored 45 points in game 1 and 33 points in game 2. How many points does he need to average in the next 5 games to score 38.5 points per game for the series?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Michael Jordan scored 38.5 points per game
    points_per_game = 38.5
    #He scored 45 points in game 1 and 33 points in game 2
    points_game_1 = 45
    points_game_2 = 33
    #He needs to average this many points in the next 5 games
    points_next_5_games = (points_game_1 + points_game_2) / 2
    return points_next_5_games

    cookies_sugar = 5
    #The answer is
    result = cookies_total - cookies_chocolate_chip
    return result

    instagram_followers = 5000
    #She has 100,000 more Twitter followers than she has Instagram followers
    twitter_followers = instagram_followers + 100000
    #She has 200,000 more Facebook followers than she has Twitter followers
    facebook_followers = twitter_followers + 200000
    #The answer is
    result = instagram_followers + twitter_followers + facebook_followers
    return result

Topic: Ninja Turtles ### Response: 
Question: There are 4 Ninja Turtles. 3 of the Ninja Turtles are 5 years old. 1 of the Ninja Turtles is 10 years old. How many years old is the average Ninja Turtle?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The number of Ninja Turtles
    num_turtles = 4
    #The number of 5-year-old turtles
    num_5_year_old_turtles = 3
    #The number of 10-year-old turtles
    num_10_year_old_turtles = 1
    #The average age of the turtles is
    result = (num_5_year_old_turtles * 5 + num_10_year_old_turtles * 10) / num_turtles
    return result

Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response:  Question: Wonder Woman has 1000 pairs of bullet-deflecting bracelets. She gives 1/3 of them to Batman. She then gives 2/5 of what's left to Superman. How many bracelets does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Wonder Woman started with 1000 pairs of bracelets
    bracelets_initial = 1000
    #She gave 1/3 of them to Batman
    bracelets_given_batman = 1 / 3 * bracelets_initial
    #She then gave 2/5 of what's left to Superman
    bracelets_given_superman = 2 / 5 * (bracelets_initial - bracelets_given_batman)
    #The answer is
    result = bracelets_initial - bracelets_given_batman - bracelets_given_superman
    return result

Topic: Ninja Turtles ### Response: 
Question: There are 2000 ninjas in New York City. 25% of them are in the Foot Clan, 10% of them are in the Turtle Clan, and the rest are in the Hamato Clan. How many ninjas are in the Hamato Clan?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of ninjas in New York City
    total_ninjas = 2000
    #Percentage of ninjas in the Foot Clan
    foot_ninjas = 0.25 * total_ninjas
    #Percentage of ninjas in the Turtle Clan
    turtle_ninjas = 0.10 * total_ninjas
    #Percentage of ninjas in the Hamato Clan
    hamato_ninjas = 1.0 - foot_ninjas - turtle_ninjas
    #The answer is
    result = total_ninjas * hamato_ninjas
    return result

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: A football team has 22 players on its roster. 4 of the players are quarterbacks, 6 are running backs, 7 are wide receivers, 2 are tight ends, and the rest are offensive linemen. How many offensive linemen are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players on the roster
    total_players = 22
    #Number of quarterbacks
    qbs = 4
    #Number of running backs
    rbs = 6
    #Number of wide receivers
    wrs = 7
    #Number of tight ends
    tes = 2
    #Number of offensive linemen
    ol = total_players - qbs - rbs - wrs - tes
    return ol
Topic: Super Mario ### Response: 
Question: In the Super Mario game, a mushroom gives the player 5 more hit points. A star gives the player 20 more hit points. A fire flower gives the player 10 more hit points. If the player has 50 hit points and then eats a mushroom, a star, and a fire flower, how many hit points does the player have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The player started with 50 hit points
    hit_points_initial = 50
    #A mushroom gives 5 more hit points
    mushroom_hit_points = 5
    #A star gives 20 more hit points
    star_hit_points = 20
    #A fire flower gives 10 more hit points
    fire_flower_hit_points = 10
    #The answer is
    result = hit_points_initial + mushroom_hit_points + star_hit_points + fire_flower_hit_points
    return result

Topic: cookies ### Response:

    cookies_per_day = 300
    #Chocolate chip cookies baked per day
    chocolate_chip_cookies = 200
    #Oatmeal raisin cookies baked per day
    oatmeal_raisin_cookies = 100
    #Chocolate chip cookies baked in 5 days

    #35 points in the second quarter
    points_second_quarter = 35
    #20 points in the third quarter
    points_third_quarter = 20
    #35 points in the fourth quarter
    points_fourth_quarter = 35
    #The answer is
    result = points_second_quarter + points_third_quarter + points_fourth_quarter
    return result

Question: Naruto has 10000 ryo. 1000 of the ryo are in 1 ryo coins, 500 of the ryo are in 5 ryo coins, and the rest of the ryo are in 10 ryo coins. How many ryo coins does Naruto have in total?

    ten_ryo_coins = total_ryo - one_ryo_coins - five_ryo_coins
    return ten_ryo_coins

Topic: Ninja Turtles ### Response: 
Question: The Ninja Turtles have 200 pizza slices. 100 of the slices are pepperoni. 100 of the slices are cheese. 50 of the slices are pepperoni and cheese. How many pizza slices are cheese only?
Solution:

    pizza_slices = 200
    #100 of the slices are pepperoni
    pepperoni_slices = 100
    #100 of the slices are cheese
    cheese_slices = 100
    #50 of the slices are pepperoni and cheese

Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response:  Question: Hello Kitty has 1000 points. She scores 200 points in 5 games. How many points does she have now?
Solution:
def solution():

    points_initial = 1000
    #She scored 200 points in 5 games
    points_per_game = 200/5
    #5 games is
    games = 5
    #She scored
    points_added = points_per_game * games
    #The answer is
    result = points_initial + points_added
    return result

Topic: basketball ### Response: 
Question: The basketball team has 20 players. 1/4 of the players are 16 years old. 1/3 of the remaining players are 17 years old. 1/5 of the remaining players are 18 years old. How many 18-year-olds are on the team?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The number of players
    total_players = 20
    #1/4 of the players are 16 years old
    sixteen_year_olds = total_players / 4
    #1/3 of the remaining players are 17 years old
    seventeen_year_olds = (total_players - sixteen_year_olds) / 3
    #1/5 of the remaining players are 18 years old
    eighteen_year_olds = (total_players - sixteen_year_olds - seventeen_year_olds) / 5
    #The answer is
    result = eighteen_year_olds
    return result

Topic: Fortnite ### Response: 
Question: There are 50 players in a Fortnite match. 20 of the players are from the United States. 10 of the players are from China. 10 of the players are from Japan. 10 of the players are from the United Kingdom. How many players are not from the United States, China, Japan, or the United Kingdom?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Number of players in the match
    num_players = 50
    #Number of players from the United States
    players_us = 20
    #Number of players from China
    players_cn = 10
    #Number of players from Japan
    players_jp = 10
    #Number of players from the United Kingdom
    players_uk = 10
    #Players who are not from the United States, China, Japan, or the United Kingdom
    players_other = num_players - players_us - players_cn - players_jp - players_uk
    return players_other

Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: 10 cheerleaders are on a team. 2 of them are seniors. 5 of them are juniors. 2 of them are sophomores. The rest are freshmen. How many cheerleaders are freshmen?
Solution:
def solution():
    #10 cheerleaders are on a team
    total_cheerleaders = 10
    #2 of them are seniors
    senior_cheerleaders = 2
    #5 of them are juniors
    junior_cheerleaders = 5
    #2 of them are sophomores
    sophomore_cheerleaders = 2
    #The answer is
    freshman_cheerleaders = total_cheerleaders - senior_cheerleaders - junior_cheerleaders - sophomore_cheerleaders
    return freshman_cheerleaders
Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response: 
Question: Wonder Woman is in a 10-day intergalactic battle. 
She fights 5 aliens on the first day, 10 aliens on the second day, and 20 aliens on each of the remaining days. How many aliens does she fight in total?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Wonder Woman fights 5 aliens on the first day
    aliens_fought_day1 = 5
    #10 aliens on the second day
    aliens_fought_day2 = 10
    #and 20 aliens on each of the remaining days
    aliens_fought_remaining_days = 20
    #There are 8 remaining days
    num_remaining_days = 10 - 2
    #The answer is
    result = aliens_fought_day1 + aliens_fought_day2 + aliens_fought_remaining_days * num_remaining_days
    return result

    setters = 2
    #3 of the players are outside hitters
    outside_hitters = 3
    #4 of the players are middle hitters
    middle_hitters = 4
    #The answer is
    result = total_players - setters - outside_hitters - middle_hitters
    return result

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: The ice cream shop has 100 scoops of ice cream. 20 of the scoops are chocolate, 30 are strawberry, and the rest are vanilla. How many scoops of ice cream are vanilla?
Solution:
def solution():

    scoops_total = 100
    #20 of the scoops are chocolate
    scoops_chocolate = 20
    #30 of the scoops are strawberry
    scoops_strawberry = 30
    #The rest are vanilla
    scoops_vanilla = scoops_total - scoops_chocolate - scoops_strawberry
    #The answer is
    result = scoops_vanilla
    return result

Question: Steph Curry made 300 three pointers this season. 150 of the three pointers were in the first half and 120 were in the second half. How many three pointers were made in the third quarter?

    total_three_pointers = 300
    #Three pointers made in the first half
    three_pointers_first_half = 150
    #Three pointers made in the second half

Topic: Minecraft ### Response: 
Question: 1000 Minecraft players were at a Minecraft tournament. 25% of the players were from the visiting team. 50% of the players were from the home team. 200 of the players were from the press. The rest of the players were from the general public. How many players were from the general public?
Solution:
def solution():
    #1000 Minecraft players were at the Minecraft tournament
    total_players = 1000
    #25% of the players were from the visiting team
    visiting_team = total_players * 0.25
    #50% of the players were from the home team
    home_team = total_players * 0.50
    #200 of the players were from the press
    press = 200
    #The rest of the players were from the general public. The answer is
    general_public = total_players - visiting_team - home_team - press
    return general_public

Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: A cheerleading squad of 12 girls and 2 boys is going to a competition. They all need to buy a new uniform. The girls' uniforms cost $100 each and the boys' uniforms cost $50 each. How much will the new uniforms cost in total?

Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 12 girls and 2 boys in the squad
    girls = 12
    boys = 2
    #Girls' uniforms cost $100 each and boys' uniforms cost $50 each
    girls_uniform_cost = 100
    boys_uniform_cost = 50
    #The total cost is
    total_cost = (girls * girls_uniform_cost) + (boys * boys_uniform_cost)
    return total_cost

Question: A cat has 9 lives. Each time a cat dies, it loses 1 life. How many times can a cat die?
Solution:
def solution():

    lives = 9
    #Each time a cat dies, it loses 1 life
    lives_lost_per_death = 1
    #The answer is

    return result

    #In the third game, he threw for 300 yards

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question:
The field hockey team at the University of British Columbia has 25 players.

How many players are from Montreal?

Solution:
def solution():

    # total players

    total_players = 25

    # players from Vancouver and Toronto

    players_from_vancouver = 10

    players_from_toronto = 7

    # players from Montreal

    players_from_montreal = total_players - players_from_vancouver - players_from_toronto

    return players_from_montreal

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response:

    #She flies for 4 hours a day
    hours_per_day = 4
    #5 days a week
    days_per_week = 5
    #4 weeks
    weeks = 4
    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: Fortnite ### Response: 
Question: A player has 200 wood, 300 stone, and 500 metal. He spends 100 wood, 200 stone, and 400 metal to build a structure. How many materials does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A player has 200 wood, 300 stone, and 500 metal
    wood = 200
    stone = 300
    metal = 500
    #He spends 100 wood, 200 stone, and 400 metal to build a structure
    wood_spent = 100
    stone_spent = 200
    metal_spent = 400
    #The answer is
    result = wood - wood_spent + stone - stone_spent + metal - metal_spent
    return result

Topic: Steph Curry ### Response: 
Question: Steph Curry is the best shooter in the NBA. He has 200 3-pointers. 50% of the 3-pointers are from the left, 30% are from the right, and the rest are from the center. How many 3-pointers has he made from the center?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry has 200 3-pointers
    three_pointers = 200
    #50% of the 3-pointers are from the left
    three_pointers_left = three_pointers * 0.5
    #30% are from the right
    three_pointers_right = three_pointers * 0.3
    #The rest are from the center
    three_pointers_center = three_pointers - three_pointers_left - three_pointers_right
    return three_pointers_center

Solution:
def solution():
    # There are 18 types of Pokémon
    pokemon_types = 18
    # The answer is
    result = pokemon_types * (pokemon_types + 1) / 2
    return result

Topic: Naruto ### Response: 
Question: Naruto has 24000 experience points. He needs 50000 experience points to get to the next level. He also needs 20000 experience points to enchant a pickaxe. How many more experience points does he need to get to the next level and enchant a pickaxe?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Naruto's experience points
    naruto_exp = 24000
    #Experience points needed for next level
    next_level_exp = 50000
    #Experience points needed to enchant a pickaxe
    enchant_exp = 20000
    #Experience points needed
    needed_exp = next_level_exp + enchant_exp
    #Naruto's experience points
    naruto_exp = 24000
    #How many more experience points does he need?
    more_exp = needed_exp - naruto_exp
    return more_exp

Topic: cats ### Response: 
Question: There are 12 cats on the table. 1/3 of them are black, 1/4 of them are white, and the rest are orange. How many orange cats are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of cats
    total_cats = 12
    #1/3 of them are black
    black_cats = total_cats / 3
    #1/4 of them are white
    white_cats = total_cats / 4
    #The rest of them are orange
    orange_cats = total_cats - black_cats - white_cats
    #The answer is
    result = orange_cats
    return result

Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response: 
Question: Wonder Woman can fly 1000 miles in 30 minutes. How many miles can she fly in 10 minutes?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Wonder Woman flies 1000 miles in 30 minutes
    miles_30_minutes = 1000
    #She flies 1000/30 = 33.33 miles per minute
    miles_per_minute = miles_30_minutes / 30
    #She can fly 33.33*10 = 333.33 miles in 10 minutes
    miles_10_minutes = miles_per_minute * 10
    return miles_10_minutes

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: 30 people are going to a pizza party. 20 of them are going to eat 3 slices of pizza, 5 of them are going to eat 5 slices of pizza, and the rest of them are going to eat 7 slices of pizza. How many slices of pizza are going to be eaten in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total people
    total_people = 30
    #20 of them are going to eat 3 slices of pizza
    three_slices_people = 20
    #5 of them are going to eat 5 slices of pizza
    five_slices_people = 5
    #The rest of them are going to eat 7 slices of pizza
    seven_slices_people = total_people - three_slices_people - five_slices_people
    #The total number of slices is
    result = three_slices_people * 3 + five_slices_people * 5 + seven_slices_people * 7

    shows_in_US = 38

A shop has 12000 ice cream cones. 30% of the cones are vanilla. 20% of the vanilla cones are sprinkled. 10% of the sprinkled cones are chocolate sprinkled. How many chocolate sprinkled cones are there?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of ice cream cones
    total_cones = 12000
    #Percentage of vanilla cones
    vanilla_percentage = 30/100
    #Percentage of sprinkled vanilla cones
    sprinkled_vanilla_percentage = 20/100
    #Percentage of chocolate sprinkled cones
    chocolate_sprinkled_percentage = 10/100
    #Calculate the number of chocolate sprinkled cones
    chocolate_sprinkled_cones = total_cones * vanilla_percentage * sprinkled_vanilla_percent

    #Chocolate chip cookies
    chocolate_chip_cookies = 3000
    #Oatmeal raisin cookies
    oatmeal_raisin_cookies = 1200
    #Peanut butter cookies are the rest
    peanut_butter_cookies = total_cookies - chocolate_chip_cookies - oatmeal_raisin_cookies
    return peanut_butter_cookies

Topic: volleyball ### Response:  Question: The volleyball team at the University of Michigan has 22 players. 5 of the players are seniors, 7 are juniors, and the rest are sophomores. How many sophomores are on the team?
Solution:

    total_players = 22
    #Number of seniors
    seniors = 5

Topic: Spiderman ### Response: 
Question: Spiderman is chasing the Green Goblin. Spiderman is 20 feet above the ground and 10 feet to the right of the Green Goblin. The Green Goblin is 10 feet above the ground and 20 feet to the right of Spiderman. How many feet are they apart?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman is 20 feet above the ground
    spiderman_height = 20
    #He is 10 feet to the right of the Green Goblin
    spiderman_x = 10
    #The Green Goblin is 10 feet above the ground
    goblin_height = 10
    #He is 20 feet to the right of Spiderman
    goblin_x = 20
    #The answer is
    result = math.sqrt(spiderman_x**2 + goblin_x**2 + spiderman_height**2 + goblin_height**2)
    return result

Topic: Ninja Turtles ### Response:  Question:  There are 100 pizzas in a pizza parlor.  Each pizza has 8 slices.  The Ninja Turtles eat 10 pizzas.  How many slices of pizza do the Ninja Turtles eat?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 100 pizzas in a pizza parlor
    pizzas_total = 100
    #Each pizza has 8 slices
    slices_per_pizza = 8
    #The Ninja Turtles eat 10 pizzas
    pizzas_eaten = 10
    #The answer is
    result = (pizzas_total * slices_per_pizza) - (pizzas_eaten * slices_per_pizza)
    return result

    #Hermione's wand is 10 inches long

Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question: 
A train leaves the station at 8:00 AM. It travels at 80 miles per hour. At 9:00 AM, another train leaves the station traveling at 60 miles per hour. If the trains are traveling in the same direction, how many miles apart will they be at 10:00 AM?

Solution:
def solution():
    # The first train leaves the station at 8:00 AM. It travels at 80 miles per hour.
    first_train_leaves = 8
    first_train_speed = 80
    # At 9:00 AM, another train leaves the station traveling at 60 miles per hour.
    second_train_leaves = 9
    second_train_speed = 60
    # The answer is
    result = first_train_speed * (first_train_leaves - second_train_leaves) - second_train_speed * (second_train_leaves - first_train_leaves)
    return result

    return result

Topic: Minecraft ### Response: 
Question: A Minecraft player has 1000 blocks of wood. 

The first player they encounter deals 15 damage. 

The second player they encounter deals 20 damage.

The third player they encounter deals 25 damage.

How much blocks of wood does the player have left?
Solution:
def solution():

    # initial blocks of wood
    wood_initial = 1000

    # damage from first player
    damage_first = 15

    # damage from second player
    damage_second = 20

    # damage from third player
    damage_third = 25

    # total damage
    total_damage = damage_first + damage_second + damage_third

    # blocks of wood left
    wood_left = wood_initial - total_damage

    return wood_left

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: There are 200 dinosaurs in a park. 75% of them are T-Rexes. 25% of the T-Rexes are male. How many male T-Rexes are in the park?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of dinosaurs
    total_dinosaurs = 200
    #Percentage of dinosaurs that are T-Rexes
    t_rex_percentage = 0.75
    #Total number of T-Rexes
    total_t_rexes = total_dinosaurs * t_rex_percentage
    #Percentage of T-Rexes that are male
    male_t_rex_percentage = 0.25
    #Total number of male T-Rexes
    total_male_t_rexes = total_t_rexes * male_t_rex_percentage
    return total_male_t_rexes
Topic: Naruto ### Response: 
Question: Naruto has 1000 gold coins. He uses 200 of them to buy a new outfit. He then uses 1/5 of the remaining gold coins to buy food. How many gold coins does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Naruto started with 1000 gold coins
    gold_coins_initial = 1000
    #He used 200 of them to buy a new outfit
    gold_coins_outfit = 200
    #He used 1/5 of the remaining gold coins to buy food
    gold_coins_food = (gold_coins_initial - gold_coins_outfit) / 5
    #The answer is
    result = gold_coins_initial - gold_coins_outfit - gold_coins_food
    return result

    #Spiderman started with 40 webs
    webs_initial = 40
    #He used 12 webs to stop a robbery
    webs_robbery = 12
    #He used 10 webs to save a cat from a tree
    webs_cat = 10
    #He used 8 webs to help an old lady cross the street

Topic: Steph Curry ### Response: 
Question: Steph Curry scored 123 points in 4 games. He scored 24 points in the first game, 19 points in the second game, 27 points in the third game, and 53 points in the fourth game. What was his average points per game?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry scored 123 points in 4 games
    total_points = 123
    #He scored 24 points in the first game
    first_game_points = 24
    #He scored 19 points in the second game
    second_game_points = 19
    #He scored 27 points in the third game
    third_game_points = 27
    #He scored 53 points in the fourth game
    fourth_game_points = 53
    #Average points per game = total points / total games
    result = total_points / 4
    return result

Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question: A train leaves New York for Chicago at 10:00 a.m. and arrives at 4:00 p.m. A train leaves Chicago for New York at 11:00 a.m. and arrives at 3:00 p.m. What is the distance between New York and Chicago?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A train leaves New York for Chicago at 10:00 a.m. and arrives at 4:00 p.m.
    train_new_york_chicago = 6
    #A train leaves Chicago for New York at 11:00 a.m. and arrives at 3:00 p.m.
    train_chicago_new_york = 4
    #The answer is
    result = train_new_york_chicago + train_chicago_new_york
    return result
Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: A volleyball team has 6 players. 3 of the players are 15 years old. 2 of the players are 16. 1 of the players is 14. How many years old is the average player on the team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Number of 15-year-old players
    players_15 = 3
    #Number of 16-year-old players
    players_16 = 2
    #Number of 14-year-old players
    players_14 = 1
    #Total number of players
    total_players = players_15 + players_16 + players_14
    #Total age of all players
    total_age = players_15 * 15 + players_16 * 16 + players_14 * 14
    #Average age of all players
    average_age = total_age / total_players
    return average_age

He buys 3 more toys. 

How many toys does the cat have now?

Solution:

  # initial number of toys
  toys_initial = 24

  # toys bought
  toys_bought = 3

  # calculate the number of toys now
  toys_now = toys_initial + toys_bought

  # return the answer
  return toys_now

Solution:

    #Batman has 1000 Batarangs
    batarangs_total = 1000
    #He has 500 more smoke Batarangs than regular Batarangs
    smoke_batarangs = batarangs_total - 500
    #He has 200 more Batarangs that can attach to walls than smoke Batarangs
    batarangs_attach_walls = smoke_batarangs + 200
    #The answer is
    result = batarangs_attach_walls
    return result

* 6 players are from New Jersey.

    total_players = 20
    #Players from New York
    ny_players = 10
    #Players from New Jersey
    nj_players = 6
    #Players from California
    ca_players = 4
    #Players not from New York, New Jersey, or California
    not_ny_nj_ca_players = total_players - ny_players - nj_players - ca_players

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: There are 100 people in line at the ice cream shop. 40 of them ordered chocolate, 30 ordered vanilla, and the rest ordered strawberry. How many people ordered strawberry?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of people in line
    total_people = 100
    #Number of people who ordered chocolate and vanilla
    chocolate = 40
    vanilla = 30
    #Number of people who ordered strawberry is the total number of people minus the number of people who ordered chocolate and vanilla
    strawberry = total_people - chocolate - vanilla
    return strawberry

Topic: Barbie ### Response: 
Question: Barbie has 120 shoes. 20% of the shoes are high heels. 40% of the shoes are sandals. The rest are sneakers. How many sneakers does Barbie have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Barbie has 120 shoes
    shoes_total = 120
    #20% of the shoes are high heels
    high_heels = shoes_total * 0.20
    #40% of the shoes are sandals
    sandals = shoes_total * 0.40
    #The rest are sneakers
    sneakers = shoes_total - high_heels - sandals
    #The answer is
    result = sneakers
    return result

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel can fly at 2000 miles per hour. She can run at 1000 miles per hour. 

If she flies for 3 hours and runs for 2 hours, how many miles has she covered?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel can fly at 2000 miles per hour
    captain_marvel_flight_speed = 2000
    #She can run at 1000 miles per hour
    captain_marvel_run_speed = 1000
    #She flies for 3 hours
    flight_hours = 3
    #She runs for 2 hours
    run_hours = 2
    #The answer is
    result = (captain_marvel_flight_speed * flight_hours) + (captain_marvel_run_speed * run_hours)
    return result

Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: The cheerleaders at the school are planning a pep rally.

How many hours will it take to make 200 pom-poms?

    total_pompoms = 200
    #Each pom-pom requires 20 minutes

    #How many hours will it take to make 200 pom-poms?

    return result

    #Leonardo ate 50 slices

    return result

Topic: basketball ### Response: 
Question: The Knicks scored 24 points in the first quarter. They scored 20 points more than that in the second quarter. They scored 10 points less than that in the third quarter. They scored 25 points in the fourth quarter. How many points did they score in total?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Knicks scored 24 points in the first quarter
    points_first_quarter = 24
    #They scored 20 points more than that in the second quarter
    points_second_quarter = points_first_quarter + 20
    #They scored 10 points less than that in the third quarter
    points_third_quarter = points_second_quarter - 10
    #They scored 25 points in the fourth quarter
    points_fourth_quarter = 25
    #The answer is
    result = points_first_quarter + points_second_quarter + points_third_quarter + points_fourth_quarter
    return result

Topic: Superman ### Response: 

Question: Superman can leap 1/8 of a mile at a time. How far can he leap in 4 minutes if he takes 5 leaps per minute?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can leap 1/8 of a mile at a time
    superman_leap_distance = 0.125
    #He takes 5 leaps per minute
    superman_leaps_per_minute = 5
    #4 minutes is 4 * 60 seconds
    superman_leaps_total = 4 * 60 * superman_leaps_per_minute
    #The answer is
    result = superman_leaps_total * superman_leap_distance
    return result

    #She withdrew 100.00 for a new outfit

    #She withdrew 250.00 for a new car

    #She withdrew 50.00 for a new house
    house_cost = 50
    #The answer is

    return result

Question: Steph Curry has 250 three pointers. 150 of them are from the left side of the court. 60 of them are from the right side of the court. The rest are from the center. How many of them are from the center?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry has 250 three pointers
    three_pointers_total = 250
    #150 of them are from the left side of the court
    three_pointers_left = 150
    #60 of them are from the right side of the court
    three_pointers_right = 60

    return three_pointers_center

Topic: cars ### Response: 
Question: A car is traveling 220 miles. It has to travel 20% of the way in the rain, 30% of the way in the snow, and 50% of the way in the sunshine. How many miles does it travel in the sunshine?

def solution():
    #The car is traveling 220 miles
    total_miles = 220
    #20% of the way is in the rain
    rain_miles = 0.2 * total_miles
    #30% of the way is in the snow
    snow_miles = 0.3 * total_miles
    #50% of the way is in the sunshine
    sunshine_miles = 0.5 * total_miles
    #The answer is
    result = sunshine_miles
    return result

    #Total diamond
    diamond = 300
    #Gold sold
    gold_sold = 20
    #Iron sold
    iron_sold = 10
    #Diamond sold

    return result

Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena Williams is a professional tennis player. She is 5 feet and 9 inches tall. 1 inch is 2.54 centimeters. How many centimeters tall is Serena Williams?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena is 5 feet 9 inches tall
    height_in_feet = 5
    height_in_inches = 9
    #1 foot is 30.48 centimeters
    foot_to_cm = 30.48
    #1 inch is 2.54 centimeters
    inch_to_cm = 2.54
    #The answer is
    result = (height_in_feet * foot_to_cm) + (height_in_inches * inch_to_cm)
    return result

Topic: Fortnite ### Response: 
Question: A player has 1000 total kills. 20% of those kills were in the first season, 10% in the second, 30% in the third, and the rest in the fourth. How many kills were in the fourth season?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total kills
    total_kills = 1000
    #Kills in the first season
    first_season_kills = total_kills * 0.20
    #Kills in the second season
    second_season_kills = total_kills * 0.10
    #Kills in the third season
    third_season_kills = total_kills * 0.30
    #Kills in the fourth season
    fourth_season_kills = total_kills - first_season_kills - second_season_kills - third_season_kills
    return fourth_season_kills

Topic: soccer ### Response: 
Question: The soccer team has 500 jerseys. 120 of the jerseys are white, 230 are red, and 150 are blue. How many jerseys are not white?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 500 jerseys
    jerseys_total = 500
    #120 of the jerseys are white
    jerseys_white = 120
    #230 of the jerseys are red
    jerseys_red = 230
    #150 of the jerseys are blue
    jerseys_blue = 150
    #The answer is
    jerseys_not_white = jerseys_total - jerseys_white

Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response: 
Question: Hello Kitty has 100 pieces of candy. She gives 20% of her candy to her friend, 30% of her candy to her sister, and 10% of her candy to her brother. How much candy does Hello Kitty have left?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total amount of candy Hello Kitty has
    total_candy = 100
    #Amount of candy Hello Kitty gives to her friend
    friend_candy = total_candy * 0.20
    #Amount of candy Hello Kitty gives to her sister
    sister_candy = total_candy * 0.30
    #Amount of candy Hello Kitty gives to her brother
    brother_candy = total_candy * 0.10
    #The answer is
    result = total_candy - friend_candy - sister_candy - brother_candy
    return result
Topic: candy ### Response: 
Question: A bag of candy has 200 pieces of candy. 100 of the pieces of candy are lollipops. 70 of the pieces of candy are gummy bears. 30 of the pieces of candy are lollipops and gummy bears. How many pieces of candy are neither lollipops nor gummy bears?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of pieces of candy
    total_candy = 200
    #Number of lollipops
    lollipops = 100
    #Number of gummy bears
    gummy_bears = 70
    #Number of pieces of candy that are both lollipops and gummy bears
    both = 30
    #The answer is
    result = total_candy - lollipops - gummy_bears + both
    return result

Topic: candy ### Response: 
Question: A candy store has 1500 lollipops. On Tuesday, 250 lollipops were sold. On Wednesday, 220 lollipops were sold. How many lollipops were left on Thursday?

Solution:

def solution():
    #The candy store started with 1500 lollipops
    lollipops_initial = 1500
    #On Tuesday, 250 lollipops were sold
    lollipops_sold_tuesday = 250
    #On Wednesday, 220 lollipops were sold
    lollipops_sold_wednesday = 220
    #The answer is
    result = lollipops_initial - lollipops_sold_tuesday - lollipops_sold_wednesday
    return result

Topic: planes ### Response: 
Question: A plane leaves New York at 10:00 AM and arrives in Los Angeles at 12:00 PM. The plane flies at an average speed of 500 mph. How long does it take for the plane to fly from New York to Los Angeles?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The plane leaves New York at 10:00 AM
    time_departure_new_york = 10
    #It arrives in Los Angeles at 12:00 PM
    time_arrival_los_angeles = 12
    #The plane flies at an average speed of 500 mph
    plane_speed = 500
    #The answer is
    result = (time_arrival_los_angeles - time_departure_new_york) / plane_speed
    return result

    turtles = 4
    #Each turtle ate 3 pizzas
    pizzas_per_turtle = 3
    #2 of the turtles ate 2 more pizzas each
    pizzas_for_2_turtles = 2 * 2

    return result

Topic: Captain America ### Response: 
Question: Captain America has 100 shields. 50 shields are in the shape of a circle, 25 are in the shape of a star, and the rest are in the shape of a triangle. How many shields are in the shape of a triangle?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain America has 100 shields
    shields_total = 100
    #50 shields are in the shape of a circle
    shields_circle = 50
    #25 shields are in the shape of a star
    shields_star = 25
    #The rest are in the shape of a triangle
    shields_triangle = shields_total - shields_circle - shields_star
    #The answer is
    result = shields_triangle
    return result

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: A candy store has 2000 chocolate bars. 30% of them are Hershey's, 20% are Cadbury, and the rest are Nestle. How many Nestle chocolate bars are there?

def solution():
    #Total chocolate bars
    total_chocolate_bars = 2000
    #Percentage of Hershey's chocolate bars
    hershey_percentage = 0.30
    #Percentage of Cadbury chocolate bars
    cadbury_percentage = 0.20
    #Percentage of Nestle chocolate bars
    nestle_percentage = 1 - hershey_percentage - cadbury_percentage
    #The number of Nestle chocolate bars is
    nestle_chocolate_bars = total_chocolate_bars * nestle_percentage
    return nestle_chocolate_bars

    slices_per_pizza = 8
    #5 pizzas are ordered
    pizzas_ordered = 5
    #3 of the pizzas are topped with mushrooms and 2 of the pizzas are topped with pepperoni

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: The U.S. field hockey team has 12 players. The German team has 3 more players. The Indian team has 25% more players than the German team. How many players are on the Indian team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The U.S. team has 12 players
    us_players = 12
    #The German team has 3 more players
    german_players = us_players + 3
    #The Indian team has 25% more players than the German team
    indian_players = german_players + (german_players * 0.25)
    #The answer is
    result = int(indian_players)
    return result

Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response: 

Question: Hello Kitty weighs 200 pounds. She eats 2000 calories a day. How long does it take for her to lose 10 pounds?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Hello Kitty weighs 200 pounds
    weight = 200
    #She eats 2000 calories a day
    calories_per_day = 2000
    #She needs to eat 1500 calories a day to lose 10 pounds
    calories_per_day_to_lose_10_pounds = 1500
    #The answer is
    result = (weight / (calories_per_day - calories_per_day_to_lose_10_pounds)) * 10
    return result
Topic: dinosaurs ### Response:

Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 250 dinosaurs in total
    dinosaurs_total = 250
    #80 of them are in the Jurassic Forest
    dinosaurs_jurassic_forest = 80
    #50 of them are in the Cretaceous Desert
    dinosaurs_cretaceous_desert = 50
    #The rest are in the Triassic Swamp. The answer is
    dinosaurs_triassic_swamp = dinosaurs_total - dinosaurs_jurassic_forest - dinosaurs_cretaceous_desert
    return dinosaurs_triassic_swamp

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: There are 10 pizza slices. 

Naruto ate 2 slices. 

Sasuke ate 3 slices. 

Sakura ate 2 slices. 

How many slices are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total slices of pizza
    total_pizza_slices = 10
    #Naruto ate 2 slices
    naruto_slices = 2
    #Sasuke ate 3 slices
    sasuke_slices = 3
    #Sakura ate 2 slices
    sakura_slices = 2
    #Total slices eaten
    total_slices_eaten = naruto_slices + sasuke_slices + sakura_slices
    #Number of slices left
    result = total_pizza_slices - total_slices_eaten
    return result

Question: Wonder Woman has 1000 followers on Instagram. 100 more people followed her on Monday, 200 more on Tuesday, 500 more on Wednesday, and 300 more on Thursday. How many followers does she have now?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Wonder Woman started with 1000 followers
    followers_initial = 1000
    #100 more people followed her on Monday
    followers_monday = 100
    #200 more on Tuesday
    followers_tuesday = 200
    #500 more on Wednesday
    followers_wednesday = 500
    #300 more on Thursday
    followers_thursday = 300
    #The answer is
    result = followers_initial + followers_monday + followers_tuesday + followers_wednesday + followers_thursday
    return result
Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: An ice cream shop has 100 flavors of ice cream. 50 of the flavors are chocolate, 30 of the flavors are vanilla, and the rest of the flavors are strawberry. How many strawberry flavors are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #An ice cream shop has 100 flavors of ice cream
    flavors_total = 100
    #50 of the flavors are chocolate, 30 of the flavors are vanilla, and the rest of the flavors are strawberry
    flavors_chocolate = 50
    flavors_vanilla = 30
    flavors_strawberry = flavors_total - flavors_chocolate - flavors_vanilla
    return flavors_strawberry

Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response: 
Question: Thor is the God of Thunder. 
He can throw his hammer 200 feet. 
If he throws his hammer 10 times, how far does his hammer travel?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Thor can throw his hammer 200 feet
    hammer_distance = 200
    #He throws his hammer 10 times
    hammer_throws = 10
    #The answer is
    result = hammer_distance * hammer_throws
    return result

Topic: LeBron James ### Response: 
Question: LeBron James has 3000 points. He scores 500 points in the first quarter, 2000 points in the second quarter, and 1000 points in the third quarter. How many points does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron James started with 3000 points
    points_initial = 3000
    #He scored 500 points in the first quarter
    points_first_quarter = 500
    #He scored 2000 points in the second quarter
    points_second_quarter = 2000
    #He scored 1000 points in the third quarter
    points_third_quarter = 1000
    #The answer is
    result = points_initial - points_first_quarter - points_second_quarter - points_third_quarter
    return result

Question: Superman is flying at 300 miles per hour. He has to fly 3,000 miles to get to the location of a meteor shower. How many hours will it take Superman to get to the meteor shower?

    #Superman's speed
    superman_speed = 300
    #Distance Superman has to travel
    superman_distance = 3000
    #The answer is
    result = superman_distance / superman_speed
    return result

    #He bought a fire flower for 100 gold coins

Question: There are 12 players on a field hockey team. 7 of the players are in 11th grade. 3 of the players are in 12th grade. 2 of the players are in 9th grade. 1 of the players is in 10th grade. How many of the players are in 11th or 12th grade?

    total_players = 12
    #7 of the players are in 11th grade
    players_11th = 7

    #2 of the players are in 9th grade
    players_9th = 2
    #1 of the players is in 10th grade
    players_10th = 1
    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizzeria sells 12-slice pizzas. 100 pizzas were sold on Monday, 200 on Tuesday, and 300 on Wednesday. How many pizza slices were sold?
Solution:
def solution():
    #12-slice pizzas were sold
    slices_per_pizza = 12
    #100 pizzas were sold on Monday, 200 on Tuesday, and 300 on Wednesday
    pizzas_sold_monday = 100
    pizzas_sold_tuesday = 200
    pizzas_sold_wednesday = 300
    #The answer is
    result = (pizzas_sold_monday + pizzas_sold_tuesday + pizzas_sold_wednesday) * slices_per_pizza
    return result
Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel is fighting a Skrull. The Skrull has 200 soldiers. 30 of them are on the ground, 60 are in the air, and the rest are in space. How many Skrull soldiers are in space?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The Skrull has 200 soldiers
    soldiers = 200
    #30 of them are on the ground
    ground_soldiers = 30
    #60 are in the air
    air_soldiers = 60
    #The rest are in space
    space_soldiers = soldiers - ground_soldiers - air_soldiers
    return space_soldiers

Topic: Pokémon ### Response: 
Question: 
Ash has 600 Pokéballs. He uses 200 of them to catch Pokémon. 
He gives away 50 of the Pokémon he catches. 
He trades 30 of the Pokémon he catches. 
How many Pokémon does Ash have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Ash has 600 Pokéballs
    pokemon_initial = 600
    #He uses 200 of them to catch Pokémon
    pokemon_used = 200
    #He gives away 50 of the Pokémon he catches
    pokemon_given_away = 50
    #He trades 30 of the Pokémon he catches
    pokemon_traded = 30
    #The answer is
    result = pokemon_initial - pokemon_used + pokemon_given_away + pokemon_traded
    return result

    money_initial = 1000000000000

    return result
Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response: 
Question: Taylor Swift has 1000 albums. 1/3 of the albums are in her car, 1/5 of the albums are in her house, and the rest are in her studio. How many albums are in her studio?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Taylor Swift has 1000 albums
    albums = 1000
    #1/3 of the albums are in her car
    albums_in_car = albums * 1/3
    #1/5 of the albums are in her house
    albums_in_house = albums * 1/5
    #The answer is
    albums_in_studio = albums - albums_in_car - albums_in_house
    return albums_in_studio

Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response: 
Question: Wonder Woman is 6'2" tall. 12" is 1 foot. How many inches is she?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Wonder Woman is 6'2" tall
    wonder_woman_height_feet = 6
    wonder_woman_height_inches = 2
    #12" is 1 foot
    feet_to_inches = 12
    #The answer is
    result = (wonder_woman_height_feet * feet_to_inches) + wonder_woman_height_inches
    return result

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: The T-Rex is the largest dinosaur.  It is 50% bigger than the Apatosaurus, which is 20% bigger than the Stegosaurus.  How many feet tall is the T-Rex? (The Stegosaurus is 20 feet tall.)

def solution():
    #The Stegosaurus is 20 feet tall
    stegosaurus_height = 20
    #The Apatosaurus is 20% bigger than the Stegosaurus
    apatosaurus_height = stegosaurus_height * 1.2
    #The T-Rex is 50% bigger than the Apatosaurus
    t_rex_height = apatosaurus_height * 1.5
    #The answer is
    result = t_rex_height
    return result

The Pink Ranger, Yellow Ranger, Black Ranger, White Ranger, Gold Ranger, Silver Ranger, and Phantom Ranger are not the original Power Rangers.     rangers_total = 10

    rangers_original = 3

    running_backs = total_players - quarterbacks - defenders - wide_receivers
    return running_backs

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: A field hockey team has 18 players. 

The coach has 18 jerseys in the locker room. 

He notices that 2/3 of the jerseys have a tear in them. 

How many jerseys does the coach have that are not torn?
Solution:
def solution():

    # number of players

    players = 18

    # number of jerseys

    jerseys = 18

    # proportion of jerseys with tears

    tears = 2/3

    # number of jerseys with tears

    torn_jerseys = jerseys * tears

    # number of jerseys without tears

    intact_jerseys = jerseys - torn_jerseys

    # the answer

    return intact_jerseys

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel can fly 500 miles per hour. She can also run 250 miles per hour. If she flies for 2 hours and runs for 3 hours, how many miles has she covered?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel can fly 500 miles per hour
    captain_marvel_flight_speed = 500
    #She can run 250 miles per hour
    captain_marvel_run_speed = 250
    #She flies for 2 hours
    flight_hours = 2
    #She runs for 3 hours
    run_hours = 3
    #The answer is
    result = (captain_marvel_flight_speed * flight_hours) + (captain_marvel_run_speed * run_hours)
    return result
Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response:

    #Hello Kitty has 5000 toys
    total_toys = 5000
    #3000 of them are cat toys
    cat_toys = 3000
    #2000 of them are dog toys
    dog_toys = 2000
    #1000 of them are both cat and dog toys
    cat_and_dog_toys = 1000
    #The number of toys that are neither cat toys nor dog toys is
    result = total_toys - cat_toys - dog_toys + cat_and_dog_toys
    return result

Solution:
def solution():
    #The T-Rex is 40 feet long
    t_rex_length = 40
    #The Brachiosaurus is 10 feet longer than the T-Rex
    brachiosaurus_length = t_rex_length + 10
    #The Apatosaurus is 10 feet shorter than the Brachiosaurus
    apatosaurus_length = brachiosaurus_length - 10
    #The Apatosaurus is
    result = apatosaurus_length
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: The volleyball team has 10 players. 3 of them are sophomores, 5 are juniors, and 2 are seniors. What is the average age of the team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The volleyball team has 10 players
    team_size = 10
    #3 of them are sophomores
    sophomores = 3
    #5 are juniors
    juniors = 5
    #2 are seniors
    seniors = 2
    #The average age is
    average_age = (sophomores*15 + juniors*16 + seniors*17) / team_size
    return average_age

Topic: cats ### Response: 
Question: 12 cats are in a room. 5 cats are white, 3 cats are black, and 4 cats are gray. How many cats are not black?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 12 cats in the room
    cats_total = 12
    #5 cats are white, 3 cats are black, and 4 cats are gray
    cats_white = 5
    cats_black = 3
    cats_gray = 4
    #The answer is
    result = cats_total - cats_black
    return result

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response:  Question: The Blue Ranger is 4 years older than the Yellow Ranger. The Red Ranger is 6 years younger than the Yellow Ranger. The Green Ranger is 3 years younger than the Red Ranger. How many years older is the Blue Ranger than the Green Ranger?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The Blue Ranger is 4 years older than the Yellow Ranger
    blue_ranger_older_than_yellow_ranger = 4
    #The Red Ranger is 6 years younger than the Yellow Ranger
    red_ranger_younger_than_yellow_ranger = 6
    #The Green Ranger is 3 years younger than the Red Ranger
    green_ranger_younger_than_red_ranger = 3
    #The answer is
    result = blue_ranger_older_than_yellow_ranger + red_ranger_younger_than_yellow_ranger + green_ranger_younger_than_red_ranger
    return result
Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question: A train leaves Los Angeles at 10:00 am and travels at 50 mph. A second train leaves New York at 12:00 pm and travels at 80 mph. How many hours after the first train leaves Los Angeles does the second train overtake the first train?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The first train leaves Los Angeles at 10:00 am and travels at 50 mph
    first_train_time = 10
    first_train_speed = 50
    #The second train leaves New York at 12:00 pm and travels at 80 mph
    second_train_time = 12
    second_train_speed = 80
    #The answer is
    result = (second_train_speed - first_train_speed) * (second_train_time - first_train_time) / second_train_speed
    return result
Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response: 
Question: Taylor Swift has 1000 concert tickets. She sells 200 tickets in the first week, 300 tickets in the second week, and 500 tickets in the third week. How many tickets does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Taylor Swift started with 1000 tickets
    tickets_initial = 1000
    #She sold 200 tickets in the first week
    tickets_sold_week1 = 200
    #She sold 300 tickets in the second week
    tickets_sold_week2 = 300
    #She sold 500 tickets in the third week
    tickets_sold_week3 = 500
    #The answer is
    result = tickets_initial - tickets_sold_week1 - tickets_sold_week2 - tickets_sold_week3
    return result

    #He gave 1 shield to Black Widow

Topic: Naruto ### Response: 
Question: 
Naruto has 3600 ryo. He spends 1000 ryo on Ramen. He spends 2000 ryo on training. How much ryo does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Naruto has 3600 ryo
    ryo_initial = 3600
    #He spends 1000 ryo on Ramen
    ryo_spent_on_ramen = 1000
    #He spends 2000 ryo on training
    ryo_spent_on_training = 2000
    #The answer is

    return result
Topic: dogs ### Response: 
Question: A dog show has 20 dogs. 10 of the dogs are German Shepherds. 5 of the dogs are Golden Retrievers. 2 of the dogs are Labrador Retrievers. The rest of the dogs are Poodles. How many Poodles are in the dog show?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A dog show has 20 dogs
    total_dogs = 20
    #10 of the dogs are German Shepherds
    german_shepherds = 10
    #5 of the dogs are Golden Retrievers
    golden_retrievers = 5
    #2 of the dogs are Labrador Retrievers
    labrador_retrievers = 2
    #The rest of the dogs are Poodles
    poodles = total_dogs - german_shepherds - golden_retrievers - labrador_retrievers
    return poodles

Topic: candy ### Response: 
Question: A bag of candy has 1000 pieces of candy. 100 of the pieces of candy are red. 200 of the pieces of candy are blue. The rest of the pieces of candy are green. How many pieces of candy are green?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A bag of candy has 1000 pieces of candy
    total_candy = 1000
    #100 of the pieces of candy are red
    red_candy = 100
    #200 of the pieces of candy are blue
    blue_candy = 200
    #The rest of the pieces of candy are green
    green_candy = total_candy - red_candy - blue_candy
    return green_candy

Question: LeBron James has 100 pairs of sneakers. 20 of them are Nike, 15 are Adidas, and 10 are Reebok. The rest of the sneakers are Converse. How many pairs of Converse sneakers does LeBron James have?
Solution:

    sneakers_total = 100
    #20 of them are Nike

    #15 are Adidas

Topic: cats ### Response: 
Question: There are 100 cats in a room. 50 cats are black. 20 cats are white. 10 cats are grey. 10 cats are orange. 10 cats are brown. How many cats are not black, white, grey, orange, or brown?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 100 cats in a room
    cats_total = 100
    #50 cats are black
    cats_black = 50
    #20 cats are white
    cats_white = 20
    #10 cats are grey
    cats_grey = 10
    #10 cats are orange
    cats_orange = 10
    #10 cats are brown
    cats_brown = 10
    #The answer is
    result = cats_total - cats_black - cats_white - cats_grey - cats_orange - cats_brown
    return result

Topic: candy ### Response: 
Question: A bag of candy has 100 pieces of candy. 50 of the pieces are chocolate. 25 of the pieces are gummy. 10 of the pieces are sour. 15 of the pieces are other types of candy. How many pieces of candy are not chocolate?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of pieces of candy
    total_candy = 100
    #Number of chocolate pieces
    chocolate_candy = 50
    #Number of gummy pieces
    gummy_candy = 25
    #Number of sour pieces
    sour_candy = 10
    #Number of other types of candy
    other_candy = 15
    #Number of non-chocolate pieces
    non_chocolate_candy = total_candy - chocolate_candy
    return non_chocolate_candy
Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: The cheer leading squad has 30 girls. 1/3 of them are freshmen. 1/3 of them are sophomores. 1/3 of them are juniors. How many cheer leaders are in each grade?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of cheer leaders
    total_cheer_leaders = 30
    #1/3 of them are freshmen
    freshmen_cheer_leaders = 1/3 * total_cheer_leaders
    #1/3 of them are sophomores
    sophomore_cheer_leaders = 1/3 * total_cheer_leaders
    #1/3 of them are juniors
    junior_cheer_leaders = 1/3 * total_cheer_leaders
    #The answer is
    result = freshmen_cheer_leaders + sophomore_cheer_leaders + junior_cheer_leaders
    return result

Topic: Fortnite ### Response: 
Question: 100 people are playing a Fortnite game. 25 of them are eliminated in the first 10 minutes. 50 of the remaining players are eliminated in the next 10 minutes. 10 more are eliminated in the next 5 minutes. How many people are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #100 people are playing
    people_playing = 100
    #25 of them are eliminated in the first 10 minutes
    elimination_10_minutes = 25
    #50 of the remaining players are eliminated in the next 10 minutes
    elimination_20_minutes = 50
    #10 more are eliminated in the next 5 minutes
    elimination_25_minutes = 10
    #The answer is
    result = people_playing - elimination_10_minutes - elimination_20_minutes - elimination_25_minutes
    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: A field hockey team has 15 players. They all need to have 2 sticks, 1 helmet, and 1 pair of pads. How many total pieces of equipment do they need?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The team has 15 players
    players = 15
    #Each player needs 2 sticks, 1 helmet, and 1 pair of pads
    sticks_per_player = 2
    helmets_per_player = 1
    pads_per_player = 1
    #The total number of each item is
    total_sticks = players * sticks_per_player
    total_helmets = players * helmets_per_player
    total_pads = players * pads_per_player
    #The total number of pieces of equipment is
    total_equipment = total_sticks + total_helmets + total_pads
    return total_equipment
Topic: cookies ### Response: 
Question: Cookies are sold in packages of 6, 12, and 18. How many packages of cookies are needed to buy 100 cookies?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The number of cookies that are needed
    cookies_needed = 100
    #The number of cookies in a package of 6
    cookies_in_a_package_of_6 = 6
    #The number of cookies in a package of 12
    cookies_in_a_package_of_12 = 12
    #The number of cookies in a package of 18
    cookies_in_a_package_of_18 = 18
    #The answer is
    result = cookies_needed / cookies_in_a_package_of_6 + cookies_needed / cookies_in_a_package_of_12 + cookies_needed / cookies_in_a_package_of_18
    return result

Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response: 
Question: Thor, the God of Thunder, is fighting against the Frost Giants. He is wielding his hammer, Mjolnir, and throws it at the Frost Giants. Mjolnir returns to Thor after 10 seconds. If Thor throws Mjolnir 5 times, how long will he be fighting against the Frost Giants?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Thor throws Mjolnir 5 times
    mjolnir_throws = 5
    #Mjolnir returns to Thor after 10 seconds
    mjolnir_return_time = 10
    #The answer is
    result = mjolnir_throws * mjolnir_return_time
    return result

Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response:  Question: Wonder Woman is in the ocean. She swims 200 meters east and 300 meters north. How far is she from the starting point?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Wonder Woman swam 200 meters east
    east_distance = 200
    #She swam 300 meters north
    north_distance = 300
    #The answer is
    result = math.sqrt(east_distance**2 + north_distance**2)
    return result

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: A football team scored 3 touchdowns and 2 field goals. Each touchdown is worth 7 points and each field goal is worth 3 points. How many points did the football team score?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A football team scored 3 touchdowns and 2 field goals
    touchdowns = 3
    field_goals = 2
    #Each touchdown is worth 7 points and each field goal is worth 3 points
    touchdown_points = 7
    field_goal_points = 3
    #The answer is
    result = touchdowns * touchdown_points + field_goals * field_goal_points
    return result

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A 12-inch pizza has 6 slices, and a 16-inch pizza has 12 slices. How many slices of pizza do you get if you buy 2 12-inch pizzas and 1 16-inch pizza?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A 12-inch pizza has 6 slices
    slices_12_inch = 6
    #A 16-inch pizza has 12 slices
    slices_16_inch = 12
    #You buy 2 12-inch pizzas and 1 16-inch pizza
    pizzas_12_inch = 2
    pizzas_16_inch = 1
    #The answer is
    result = pizzas_12_inch * slices_12_inch + pizzas_16_inch * slices_16_inch
    return result

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizza place has 1000 slices of pizza. 
It sells 200 slices of pizza. 
Then, it sells 100 more slices of pizza. 
How many slices of pizza does the pizza place have left?
Solution:

    #The pizza place started with 1000 slices of pizza
    pizza_slices_initial = 1000
    #It sold 200 slices of pizza
    pizza_slices_sold_1 = 200
    #It sold 100 more slices of pizza
    pizza_slices_sold_2 = 100
    #The answer is
    result = pizza_slices_initial - pizza_slices_sold_1 - pizza_slices_sold_2
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response: 
Question: 10 dogs are in the park. 2 of them are black labs. 3 of them are golden retrievers. 2 of them are rottweilers. 3 of them are beagles. How many of the dogs are not black labs, golden retrievers, rottweilers, or beagles?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total dogs
    total_dogs = 10
    #Black labs
    black_labs = 2
    #Golden retrievers
    golden_retrievers = 3
    #Rottweilers
    rottweilers = 2
    #Beagles
    beagles = 3
    #Dogs that are not black labs, golden retrievers, rottweilers, or beagles
    other_dogs = total_dogs - black_labs - golden_retrievers - rottweilers - beagles
    return other_dogs

Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: The cheer team has 10 members. 5 of the cheerleaders are 15 years old. 4 of the cheerleaders are 16 years old. 1 of the cheerleaders is 17 years old. What is the average age of the cheerleaders?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The number of cheerleaders
    cheerleaders = 10
    #The number of 15-year-old cheerleaders
    cheerleaders_15 = 5
    #The number of 16-year-old cheerleaders
    cheerleaders_16 = 4
    #The number of 17-year-old cheerleaders
    cheerleaders_17 = 1
    #The total age of all cheerleaders
    total_age = (cheerleaders_15 * 15) + (cheerleaders_16 * 16) + (cheerleaders_17 * 17)
    #The average age is
    average_age = total_age / cheerleaders

Topic: football ### Response:  Question: A football team has 53 players. 22 of them are on offense, 21 of them are on defense, and 10 of them are on special teams. How many players are not on offense, defense, or special teams?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A football team has 53 players
    total_players = 53
    #22 of them are on offense
    offense = 22
    #21 of them are on defense
    defense = 21
    #10 of them are on special teams
    special_teams = 10
    #The answer is
    result = total_players - offense - defense - special_teams
    return result

Question: Black Panther has 1000 vibranium ingots. 1/3 of the vibranium ingots are used to make vibranium weapons, and 1/5 of the vibranium ingots used to make vibranium weapons are also used to make vibranium armor.  How many vibranium ingots are used to make vibranium armor?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Black Panther has 1000 vibranium ingots
    vibranium_ingots = 1000
    #1/3 of the vibranium ingots are used to make vibranium weapons
    vibranium_weapons = vibranium_ingots / 3
    #1/5 of the vibranium ingots used to make vibranium weapons are also used to make vibranium armor
    vibranium_armor = vibranium_weapons / 5

Topic: unicorns ### Response: 
Question: 50 unicorns and 30 dragons were in a magical land. 20 unicorns and 10 dragons left the land. 15 new unicorns and 12 new dragons arrived. How many unicorns and dragons are in the land now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Initial number of unicorns
    unicorns_initial = 50
    #Initial number of dragons
    dragons_initial = 30
    #Unicorns and dragons that left
    unicorns_left = 20
    dragons_left = 10
    #New unicorns and dragons that arrived
    unicorns_arrived = 15
    dragons_arrived = 12
    #The answer is
    result = (unicorns_initial - unicorns_left + unicorns_arrived, dragons_initial - dragons_left + dragons_arrived)
    return result

Topic: Naruto ### Response:  Question: Naruto is training to become a ninja. He trains 30 hours per week. He trains for 6 hours on Monday, 7 hours on Tuesday, 8 hours on Wednesday, 9 hours on Thursday, and 10 hours on Friday. How many hours does he train on Saturday and Sunday?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Naruto trains 30 hours per week
    hours_per_week = 30
    #He trains for 6 hours on Monday
    hours_monday = 6
    #7 hours on Tuesday
    hours_tuesday = 7
    #8 hours on Wednesday
    hours_wednesday = 8
    #9 hours on Thursday
    hours_thursday = 9
    #and 10 hours on Friday
    hours_friday = 10
    #The answer is
    result = hours_per_week - hours_monday - hours_tuesday - hours_wednesday - hours_thursday - hours_friday
    return result

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel is on a mission to save the world. She has to run 3000 meters to the first checkpoint. Then she has to run 3/4 as far to the second checkpoint. How many meters does she have to run in total?
Solution:

    #The first checkpoint is 3000 meters away
    first_checkpoint = 3000
    #The second checkpoint is 3/4 as far as the first
    second_checkpoint = first_checkpoint * (3/4)
    #The total distance is
    total_distance = first_checkpoint + second_checkpoint
    return total_distance

Topic: candy ### Response: 
Question: There are 500 pieces of candy in a jar. 1/4 of the candy is red. 1/3 of the candy is green. 1/6 of the candy is blue. What fraction of the candy is not red, green, or blue?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 500 pieces of candy in a jar
    total_candy = 500
    #1/4 of the candy is red
    red_candy = total_candy / 4
    #1/3 of the candy is green
    green_candy = total_candy / 3
    #1/6 of the candy is blue
    blue_candy = total_candy / 6
    #The answer is
    result = total_candy - red_candy - green_candy - blue_candy
    return result
Topic: trains ### Response:

Solution:

    #10-car train is 1200 feet long
    train_10_car = 1200
    #15-car train is 1800 feet long
    train_15_car = 1800
    #20-car train will be
    train_20_car = (1800 - 1200) / (15 - 10) * 20
    return train_20_car

3 of the girls are seniors. 

How many girls are not freshmen, sophomores, juniors, or seniors?
Solution:

    total_girls = 12
    #Number of girls who are freshmen
    freshmen_girls = 3
    #Number of girls who are sophomores
    sophomore_girls = 4
    #Number of girls who are juniors
    junior_girls = 2
    #Number of girls who are seniors

    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel has 3000 gold bricks. She uses 1000 of them to build a mansion. She then uses 1/5 of the remaining gold bricks to build a laboratory. How many gold bricks does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel started with 3000 gold bricks
    gold_bricks_initial = 3000
    #She used 1000 of them to build a mansion
    gold_bricks_mansion = 1000
    #She used 1/5 of the remaining gold bricks to build a laboratory
    gold_bricks_laboratory = (gold_bricks_initial - gold_bricks_mansion) / 5
    #The answer is
    result = gold_bricks_initial - gold_bricks_mansion - gold_bricks_laboratory
    return result

Topic: trains ### Response:  Question: A train leaves New York City at 10:00 AM and travels at 60 miles per hour. Another train leaves Los Angeles at 9:00 AM and travels at 70 miles per hour. The distance between New York City and Los Angeles is 2500 miles. How long will it take for the trains to meet?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The distance between New York City and Los Angeles is 2500 miles
    distance = 2500
    #The first train leaves New York City at 10:00 AM and travels at 60 miles per hour
    time_train_1_departs = 10
    speed_train_1 = 60
    #The second train leaves Los Angeles at 9:00 AM and travels at 70 miles per hour
    time_train_2_departs = 9
    speed_train_2 = 70
    #The answer is
    result = distance / (speed_train_1 + speed_train_2)
    return result

Solution:
def solution():
    #Initial number of Death Eaters
    initial_death_eaters = 40
    #10 more Death Eaters apparate into the battle
    more_death_eaters = 10
    #Half of the Death Eaters are defeated
    defeated_death_eaters = (initial_death_eaters + more_death_eaters) / 2
    #The answer is
    result = (initial_death_eaters + more_death_eaters) - defeated_death_eaters
    return result

Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena Williams is the #1 tennis player in the world. 5000 people come to each of her matches. She has 10 matches a year. How many people come to her matches in 5 years?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams has 10 matches a year
    matches_per_year = 10
    #5000 people come to each match
    people_per_match = 5000
    #She has 10 matches a year. The answer is

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: The 49ers and the Rams are playing a football game. 

In the first half, the 49ers scored 14 points. 

In the second half, the 49ers scored 10 more points than the Rams, who scored 24. 

How many points did the 49ers score in the game?

Solution:
def solution():
    # 49ers' score in the first half
    first_half_score = 14

    # Rams' score in the second half
    rams_second_half_score = 24

    # 49ers' score in the second half is 10 more than the Rams'
    second_half_score = rams_second_half_score + 10

    # 49ers' total score is the sum of their first and second half scores
    total_score = first_half_score + second_half_score

    return total_score

    total_players = 12
    #16-year-old players
    sixteen_year_old = 5
    #17-year-old players
    seventeen_year_old = 3
    #18-year-old players
    eighteen_year_old = 2
    #15-year-old players
    fifteen_year_old = total_players - sixteen_year_old - seventeen_year_old - eighteen_year_old
    return fifteen_year_old

    total_titles = 23
    #14 of them are in singles

    #13 of them are in doubles

    #The rest are in mixed doubles

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: A baker bakes 100 cookies. He sells 30 on Monday, 20 on Tuesday, and 20 on Wednesday. He bakes 20 more on Thursday. How many cookies does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The baker started with 100 cookies
    cookies_initial = 100
    #He sold 30 on Monday, 20 on Tuesday, and 20 on Wednesday
    cookies_sold_monday = 30
    cookies_sold_tuesday = 20
    cookies_sold_wednesday = 20
    #He baked 20 more on Thursday
    cookies_baked_thursday = 20
    #The answer is
    result = cookies_initial - cookies_sold_monday - cookies_sold_tuesday - cookies_sold_wednesday + cookies_baked_thursday
    return result
