Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: A football team is on a 5-game winning streak. 
They won the first 3 games by a score of 21 each. 
They won the 4th game by a score of 17. 
They won the 5th game by a score of 27. 
What was their average number of points scored per game?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The team won 5 games
    games = 5
    #They won the first 3 games by a score of 21 each
    first_3_games = 3 * 21
    #They won the 4th game by a score of 17
    fourth_game = 17
    #They won the 5th game by a score of 27
    fifth_game = 27
    #The total points is
    total_points = first_3_games + fourth_game + fifth_game
    #The answer is
    result = total_points / games
    return result

Topic: Minecraft ### Response: 
Question: In Minecraft, a zombie has 20 health. It loses 3 health when a player hits it with a sword. It loses 5 health when a player hits it with an axe. It loses 8 health when a player hits it with a bow. How many times does a player have to hit a zombie with a bow to kill it?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A zombie has 20 health
    zombie_health = 20
    #It loses 3 health when a player hits it with a sword
    zombie_health_loss_sword = 3
    #It loses 5 health when a player hits it with an axe
    zombie_health_loss_axe = 5
    #It loses 8 health when a player hits it with a bow
    zombie_health_loss_bow = 8
    #The answer is
    result = zombie_health / zombie_health_loss_bow
    return result

Topic: Black Panther ### Response: 
Question: The Black Panther movie made $1.3 billion dollars. 20% of the revenue came from the United States, and 10% came from China. How much revenue came from the rest of the world?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The Black Panther movie made $1.3 billion dollars
    total_revenue = 1.3 * 1000000000
    #20% of the revenue came from the United States
    revenue_us = total_revenue * 0.20
    #10% came from China
    revenue_china = total_revenue * 0.10
    #The answer is
    result = total_revenue - revenue_us - revenue_china
    return result

    #4 unicorns are eating glitter

Topic: basketball ### Response: 
Question: The 5-man basketball team of the A-Town High School has 72 points in total. 3 of the players have 12 points each. 1 of the players has 8 points. 1 of the players has 6 points. How many points does the 5th player have?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total points
    total_points = 72
    #3 players have 12 points each
    three_players_points = 3 * 12
    #1 player has 8 points
    one_player_points_8 = 8
    #1 player has 6 points
    one_player_points_6 = 6
    #The answer is
    result = total_points - three_players_points - one_player_points_8 - one_player_points_6
    return result
Topic: cars ### Response:  Question: 500 cars are in a parking lot. 200 of the cars are Hondas, 150 are Toyotas, and the rest are Nissans. How many Nissans are there?

def solution():
    #500 cars are in a parking lot
    cars_total = 500
    #200 of the cars are Hondas
    hondas = 200
    #150 are Toyotas
    toyotas = 150
    #The rest are Nissans. The answer is
    nissans = cars_total - hondas - toyotas
    return nissans

    result = galleons - days * 2

Topic: Steph Curry ### Response: 
Question: Steph Curry made 33% of his shots in the first half and 50% of his shots in the second half. If he made 20 shots in the first half, how many shots did he make in the second half?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry made 33% of his shots in the first half
    first_half_shots = 33
    #He made 50% of his shots in the second half
    second_half_shots = 50
    #He made 20 shots in the first half
    first_half_shots_made = 20
    #The answer is
    result = first_half_shots_made * (second_half_shots/first_half_shots)
    return result

    slices = 12
    #3/4 of the slices are topped with pepperoni
    pepperoni_slices = slices * 3/4
    #2/3 of the slices topped with pepperoni are also topped with mushrooms
    mushroom_slices = pepperoni_slices * 2/3

    return result

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question:
A Tyrannosaurus Rex is chasing a herd of Triceratops. The Tyrannosaurus Rex can run 20 miles per hour. The Triceratops can run 10 miles per hour. The Tyrannosaurus Rex is 500 yards behind the Triceratops. How long will it take the Tyrannosaurus Rex to catch up to the Triceratops?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The Tyrannosaurus Rex can run 20 miles per hour
    tyrannosaurus_rex_speed = 20
    #The Triceratops can run 10 miles per hour
    triceratops_speed = 10
    #The Tyrannosaurus Rex is 500 yards behind the Triceratops
    distance_behind = 500
    #The answer is
    result = distance_behind / (tyrannosaurus_rex_speed - triceratops_speed)
    return result

Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question:
There are two trains, A and B. Train A leaves New York at 10:00 AM, and travels at 50 miles per hour. Train B leaves New York at 10:30 AM, and travels at 60 miles per hour. How far from New York will the trains meet?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Train A leaves New York at 10:00 AM
    train_a_leaves = 10
    #Train B leaves New York at 10:30 AM
    train_b_leaves = 10.5
    #Train A travels at 50 miles per hour
    train_a_speed = 50
    #Train B travels at 60 miles per hour
    train_b_speed = 60
    #The answer is
    result = train_a_speed * (train_b_leaves - train_a_leaves) / (train_a_speed - train_b_speed)
    return result

Topic: Harry Potter ### Response: 
Question: Harry Potter is in the middle of a heated battle. He is in the final 10, and he has 150 HP. 

The first player he encounters deals 15 damage. 

The second player he encounters deals 20 damage.

The third player he encounters deals 25 damage.

How much HP does Harry Potter have left?
Solution:
def solution():

    # initial HP
    hp_initial = 150

    # damage from first player
    damage_first = 15

    # damage from second player
    damage_second = 20

    # damage from third player
    damage_third = 25

    # total damage
    total_damage = damage_first + damage_second + damage_third

    # HP left
    hp_left = hp_initial - total_damage

    return hp_left
Topic: Iron Man ### Response:

    #Total number of suits
    total_suits = 50
    #Number of suits in the lab
    suits_in_lab = 30
    #Number of suits in the garage
    suits_in_garage = 10
    #Number of suits in the bunker is the total number of suits minus the number of suits in the lab and garage
    suits_in_bunker = total_suits - suits_in_lab - suits_in_garage
    return suits_in_bunker

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: In a field hockey match, the home team, Chelsea, scored 25 goals. The away team, Arsenal, scored 20. 5 of Arsenal's goals were disallowed. How many more goals did Chelsea score than Arsenal?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Chelsea scored 25 goals
    chelsea_goals = 25
    #Arsenal scored 20 goals
    arsenal_goals = 20
    #5 of Arsenal's goals were disallowed
    arsenal_disallowed_goals = 5
    #Arsenal's disallowed goals don't count, so they actually scored
    arsenal_goals_actual = arsenal_goals - arsenal_disallowed_goals
    #The answer is
    result = chelsea_goals - arsenal_goals_actual
    return result

Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response:  Question: Thor is fighting the Frost Giants. There are 100 of them. Thor defeats 1/4 of them with his mighty hammer. He defeats 1/2 of the remaining Frost Giants with his lightning. How many Frost Giants does Thor defeat in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of Frost Giants
    total_frost_giants = 100
    #Thor defeats 1/4 of them with his mighty hammer
    frost_giants_defeated_by_hammer = total_frost_giants / 4
    #He defeats 1/2 of the remaining Frost Giants with his lightning
    frost_giants_defeated_by_lightning = (total_frost_giants - frost_giants_defeated_by_hammer) / 2
    #The answer is
    result = frost_giants_defeated_by_hammer + frost_giants_defeated_by_lightning
    return
Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: The volleyball team has 12 players. 4 of the players are seniors. 3 of the players are juniors. 4 of the players are sophomores. 1 of the players is a freshman. How many of the players are not seniors?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The volleyball team has 12 players
    players = 12
    #4 of the players are seniors
    seniors = 4
    #3 of the players are juniors
    juniors = 3
    #4 of the players are sophomores
    sophomores = 4
    #1 of the players is a freshman
    freshman = 1
    #The answer is
    result = players - seniors - juniors - sophomores - freshman
    return result

    #Captain America has 50 throwing shields
    shields_total = 50
    #25 of them are in his shield belt
    shields_belt = 25
    #15 of them are in his shield backpack
    shields_backpack = 15
    #5 of them are in his shield suitcase
    shields_suitcase = 5
    #The answer is
    result = shields_total - shields_belt - shields_backpack - shields_suitcase
    return result

Question: A cat has 9 lives. 3 of the lives are good lives and 2 of the lives are bad lives. 2 of the lives are both good and bad. 2 of the lives are neither good nor bad. How many of the lives are good or bad?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A cat has 9 lives
    lives = 9
    #3 of the lives are good lives
    good_lives = 3
    #2 of the lives are bad lives
    bad_lives = 2
    #2 of the lives are both good and bad
    both_good_bad_lives = 2
    #2 of the lives are neither good nor bad
    neither_good_nor_bad_lives = 2
    #The answer is
    result = good_lives + bad_lives + both_good_bad_lives
    return result

Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response: 
Question: Patrick Mahomes has 300 footballs. 100 of them are for practice, and the rest are for games. 50 of the footballs for games are in his house, and the rest are in his car. How many footballs for games are in his car?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Patrick Mahomes has 300 footballs
    total_footballs = 300
    #100 of them are for practice
    practice_footballs = 100
    #The rest are for games
    game_footballs = total_footballs - practice_footballs
    #50 of the footballs for games are in his house
    game_footballs_in_house = 50
    #The rest are in his car
    game_footballs_in_car = game_footballs - game_footballs_in_house
    #The answer is
    result = game_footballs_in_car
    return result

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel has 2000 photon blasts. She uses 1/3 of her photon blasts to defeat Ronan. She then uses 200 photon blasts to defeat Yon-Rogg. How many photon blasts does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel has 2000 photon blasts
    photon_blasts_initial = 2000
    #She uses 1/3 of her photon blasts to defeat Ronan
    photon_blasts_ronan = 1 / 3 * photon_blasts_initial
    #She then uses 200 photon blasts to defeat Yon-Rogg
    photon_blasts_yon_rogg = 200
    #The answer is
    result = photon_blasts_initial - photon_blasts_ronan - photon_blasts_yon_rogg
    return result

    #He scored 3 points in the first quarter
    first_quarter_points = 3
    #5 points in the second quarter
    second_quarter_points = 5
    #4 points in the third quarter
    third_quarter_points = 4
    #and 5 points in the fourth quarter

    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response:  Question: 100 dogs are in the shelter. 50% of the dogs are adopted. 50 more dogs are brought to the shelter. How many dogs are in the shelter now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #100 dogs are in the shelter
    dogs_initial = 100
    #50% of the dogs are adopted
    dogs_adopted = 0.50 * dogs_initial
    #50 more dogs are brought to the shelter
    dogs_added = 50
    #The answer is
    result = dogs_initial - dogs_adopted + dogs_added
    return result

    time_depart_chicago = 5
    #It arrives in Los Angeles at 10:00 PM
    time_arrive_LA = 22
    #The train leaves Los Angeles at 10:00 AM
    time_depart_LA = 10
    #It arrives in Chicago at 5:00 PM

    #The answer is

    return result

Solution:

    #LeBron James has played in 100 games
    games = 100
    #He has scored 25 points in 20 of those games
    points_25 = 25
    #He has scored 30 points in 30 of those games
    points_30 = 30
    #He has scored 40 points in 50 of those games
    points_40 = 40
    #The answer is
    result = games * (points_25 * 20 + points_30 * 30 + points_40 * 50)
    return result

Question: Batman can throw 50 batarangs in 5 seconds. How many batarangs can he throw in 10 seconds?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Batman can throw 50 batarangs in 5 seconds
    batarangs_in_5_seconds = 50
    #So, in 10 seconds, he can throw
    batarangs_in_10_seconds = batarangs_in_5_seconds * 2
    return batarangs_in_10_seconds
Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response: 
Question: Thor is a 2,000-pound pig.  He eats 20 pounds of food a day.  How much food does he need for 30 days?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Thor weighs 2000 pounds
    thor_weight = 2000
    #He eats 20 pounds of food a day
    food_per_day = 20
    #He needs to eat for 30 days
    days = 30
    #The answer is
    result = thor_weight * food_per_day * days
    return result

Topic: Superman ### Response: 
Question: Superman can fly at 1000 miles per hour. How many hours will it take him to fly 1000 miles?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can fly at 1000 miles per hour
    superman_speed = 1000
    #How many hours will it take him to fly 1000 miles?
    superman_hours = 1000 / superman_speed
    return superman_hours
Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response: 
Question: In the 2020 season, Patrick Mahomes threw for 4740 yards. In the 2021 season, he threw for 4839 yards. In the 2022 season, he threw for 5250 yards. How many yards did he throw for in total in the 3 seasons?
Solution:
def solution():
    #In the 2020 season, Patrick Mahomes threw for 4740 yards
    yards_thrown_2020 = 4740
    #In the 2021 season, he threw for 4839 yards
    yards_thrown_2021 = 4839
    #In the 2022 season, he threw for 5250 yards
    yards_thrown_2022 = 5250
    #The answer is
    result = yards_thrown_2020 + yards_thrown_2021 + yards_thrown_2022
    return result

Question: The Black Panther has 5000 vibranium-powered suits. 1000 of the suits are in Wakanda, 2000 are in the United States, and 1000 are in South Korea. 500 more suits are in Wakanda. How many suits are in the United States and South Korea?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of suits
    total_suits = 5000
    #Suit in Wakanda
    suits_in_wakanda = 1000
    #Suit in United States
    suits_in_us = 2000
    #Suit in South Korea
    suits_in_sk = 1000
    #Suit in Wakanda
    suits_in_wakanda_more = 500
    #The answer is
    result = suits_in_us + suits_in_sk
    return result
Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Iron Man is 1000 years old. His father is 100 years older than he is. His grandfather is 100 years older than his father. How old is Iron Man's grandfather?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man is 1000 years old
    iron_man_age = 1000
    #Iron Man's father is 100 years older than he is
    iron_man_father_age = iron_man_age + 100
    #Iron Man's grandfather is 100 years older than his father
    iron_man_grandfather_age = iron_man_father_age + 100
    #The answer is
    result = iron_man_grandfather_age
    return result
Topic: Barbie ### Response: 
Question: Barbie has 1000 Ken dolls. She has 200 more Ken dolls than GI Joe dolls. She has 300 more GI Joe dolls than He-Man dolls. How many He-Man dolls does Barbie have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Barbie has 1000 Ken dolls
    ken_dolls = 1000
    #She has 200 more Ken dolls than GI Joe dolls
    gi_joe_dolls = ken_dolls - 200
    #She has 300 more GI Joe dolls than He-Man dolls
    he_man_dolls = gi_joe_dolls - 300
    #The answer is
    result = he_man_dolls
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response:  Question: A volleyball team is made up of 12 players. 8 of the players are from the US and the rest are from Canada. 3 of the Canadian players are from Toronto, and the rest are from Vancouver. How many players are from Vancouver?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The team has 12 players
    total_players = 12
    #8 of them are from the US
    us_players = 8
    #The rest are from Canada
    canada_players = total_players - us_players
    #3 of the Canadian players are from Toronto
    toronto_players = 3
    #The rest are from Vancouver
    vancouver_players = canada_players - toronto_players
    #The answer is
    result = vancouver_players
    return result

Topic: Spiderman ### Response: 
Question: Spiderman has 100 web-shooters. He used 20 on the Green Goblin, 25 on the Lizard, and 35 on the Sinister Six. How many web-shooters does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman started with 100 web-shooters
    web_shooters_initial = 100
    #He used 20 on the Green Goblin
    web_shooters_used_goblin = 20
    #He used 25 on the Lizard
    web_shooters_used_lizard = 25
    #He used 35 on the Sinister Six
    web_shooters_used_six = 35
    #The answer is
    result = web_shooters_initial - web_shooters_used_goblin - web_shooters_used_lizard - web_shooters_used_six
    return result
Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response: 
Question: Patrick Mahomes is a professional football player. He is 6 feet and 3 inches tall. 1 inch is 2.54 centimeters. How many centimeters tall is Patrick Mahomes?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Patrick is 6 feet 3 inches tall
    height_in_feet = 6
    height_in_inches = 3
    #1 foot is 30.48 centimeters
    foot_to_cm = 30.48
    #1 inch is 2.54 centimeters
    inch_to_cm = 2.54
    #The answer is
    result = (height_in_feet * foot_to_cm) + (height_in_inches * inch_to_cm)
    return result

Topic: cookies ### Response: 
Question: A cookie jar contains 100 cookies. 25 cookies are eaten on Monday, 50 cookies are eaten on Tuesday, and 15 cookies are eaten on Wednesday. How many cookies are left in the jar?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The initial number of cookies
    cookies_initial = 100
    #The number of cookies eaten on Monday
    cookies_eaten_monday = 25
    #The number of cookies eaten on Tuesday
    cookies_eaten_tuesday = 50
    #The number of cookies eaten on Wednesday
    cookies_eaten_wednesday = 15
    #The answer is
    result = cookies_initial - cookies_eaten_monday - cookies_eaten_tuesday - cookies_eaten_wednesday
    return result
Topic: Super Mario ### Response: 
Question: In Super Mario, each mushroom gives 5 health points and each star gives 20. 
If Mario has 30 health points and he eats 4 mushrooms and 2 stars, how many health points does he have now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Mario's initial health points
    initial_health = 30
    #Health points from mushrooms
    mushroom_health = 4 * 5
    #Health points from stars
    star_health = 2 * 20
    #The answer is
    result = initial_health + mushroom_health + star_health
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: The volleyball team has 12 players. 8 players are on the court and 4 are on the bench. How many players are on the bench?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The volleyball team has 12 players
    players_total = 12
    #8 players are on the court
    players_court = 8
    #4 are on the bench
    players_bench = players_total - players_court
    return players_bench
Topic: planes ### Response: 
Question: There are 10 airplanes at the airport. 3 are government planes, 4 are commercial airliners, and the rest are private planes. How many are private planes?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 10 airplanes at the airport
    total_airplanes = 10
    #3 are government planes
    government_planes = 3
    #4 are commercial airliners
    commercial_airliners = 4
    #The rest are private planes
    private_planes = total_airplanes - government_planes - commercial_airliners
    return private_planes
Topic: cookies ### Response: 
Question: 2000 cookies are baked every day. 1500 of them are chocolate chip. How many of them are not chocolate chip?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of cookies
    total_cookies = 2000
    #Number of chocolate chip cookies
    chocolate_chip = 1500
    #Number of cookies that are not chocolate chip
    not_chocolate_chip = total_cookies - chocolate_chip
    return not_chocolate_chip

Topic: Steph Curry ### Response: 
Question: Steph Curry has 1200 3-pointers. 400 of them are from the right side of the court, 400 are from the left side of the court, and 200 are from the top of the key. How many 3-pointers does Steph Curry have from the left side of the court?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry has 1200 3-pointers
    three_pointers_total = 1200
    #400 of them are from the right side of the court
    three_pointers_right_side = 400
    #400 are from the left side of the court
    three_pointers_left_side = 400
    #200 are from the top of the key
    three_pointers_top_key = 200
    #The answer is
    result = three_pointers_total - three_pointers_right_side - three_pointers_top_key
    return result

Topic: Spiderman ### Response: 
Question: Spiderman, the superhero, can shoot 10 webs per minute. He used 3 webs to catch a criminal, 5 webs to stop a speeding car, and 2 webs to save a kitten. How many webs does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman can shoot 10 webs per minute
    webs_per_minute = 10
    #He used 3 webs to catch a criminal, 5 webs to stop a speeding car, and 2 webs to save a kitten.
    webs_used = 3 + 5 + 2
    #The answer is
    result = webs_per_minute - webs_used
    return result

Topic: Black Panther ### Response: 
Question: Black Panther has 300 vibranium daggers. 50 of the daggers are 10 inches long. 124 of the daggers are 20 inches long. 60 of the daggers are 30 inches long. How many inches of vibranium daggers does Black Panther have?
Solution:
def solution():
    # Black Panther has 300 vibranium daggers
    daggers = 300
    # 50 of the daggers are 10 inches long
    daggers_10 = 50
    # 124 of the daggers are 20 inches long
    daggers_20 = 124
    # 60 of the daggers are 30 inches long
    daggers_30 = 60
    # The answer is
    result = daggers_10 * 10 + daggers_20 * 20 + daggers_30 * 30
    return result
Topic: basketball ### Response: 
Question: In the 2021-2022 season, Steph Curry made 288 three-point shots. He made 42% of his three-point shots. How many three-point shots did he attempt?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Steph Curry made 288 three-point shots
    three_point_shots_made = 288
    #He made 42% of his three-point shots
    three_point_shot_percentage = 42
    #The answer is
    result = three_point_shots_made / (three_point_shot_percentage / 100)
    return result

Topic: Ninja Turtles ### Response: 

Question: There are 12 ninja turtles. 6 of the turtles are named after artists. 3 of the turtles are named after musicians. 2 of the turtles are named after both artists and musicians. How many turtles are named after neither artists nor musicians?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of turtles
    total_turtles = 12
    #Turtles named after artists
    artist_turtles = 6
    #Turtles named after musicians
    musician_turtles = 3
    #Turtles named after both artists and musicians
    both_turtles = 2
    #Turtles named after neither artists nor musicians is
    neither_turtles = total_turtles - artist_turtles - musician_turtles + both_turtles
    return neither_turtles

Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Iron Man can fly 300 miles in 20 minutes. How far can he fly in 1 hour?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man can fly 300 miles in 20 minutes
    miles_per_20_minutes = 300
    #1 hour is 60 minutes
    minutes_1_hour = 60
    #The answer is
    result = (miles_per_20_minutes / 20) * minutes_1_hour
    return result

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: The T-Rex is the largest dinosaur.  It is 50% bigger than the Apatosaurus, which is 20% bigger than the Stegosaurus.  How many feet tall is the T-Rex? (The Stegosaurus is 20 feet tall.)
Solution:
def solution():
    #The Stegosaurus is 20 feet tall
    stegosaurus_height = 20
    #The Apatosaurus is 20% bigger than the Stegosaurus
    apatosaurus_height = stegosaurus_height * 1.2
    #The T-Rex is 50% bigger than the Apatosaurus
    t_rex_height = apatosaurus_height * 1.5
    #The answer is
    result = t_rex_height
    return result

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: A football team scored 21 points in the first quarter, 14 points in the second quarter, 17 points in the third quarter, and 7 points in the fourth quarter. How many points did they score in the game?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The team scored 21 points in the first quarter
    points_first_quarter = 21
    #14 points in the second quarter
    points_second_quarter = 14
    #17 points in the third quarter
    points_third_quarter = 17
    #and 7 points in the fourth quarter
    points_fourth_quarter = 7
    #The answer is
    result = points_first_quarter + points_second_quarter + points_third_quarter + points_fourth_quarter
    return result

    #The number of water type Pokémon

    #The answer is

Topic: cats ### Response: 
Question: There are 25 cats in a room. 10 of them are black. 12 of them are white. How many cats are not black or white?

    cats_initial = 25

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question:

A T-Rex is chasing a velociraptor. 

The T-Rex is 100 feet away from the velociraptor. 

The T-Rex can run at 17 miles per hour. 

The velociraptor can run at 24 miles per hour. 

How long will it take the T-Rex to catch the velociraptor?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The T-Rex is 100 feet away from the velociraptor
    distance_between_dinos = 100
    #The T-Rex can run at 17 miles per hour
    t_rex_speed = 17
    #The velociraptor can run at 24 miles per hour
    velociraptor_speed = 24
    #The answer is
    result = distance_between_dinos / (t_rex_speed - velociraptor_speed)
    return result
Topic: Captain America ### Response: 
Question: Captain America has 25 shields. He uses 5 of them in the first mission, and 4 of them in the second mission. 2 of the shields are damaged and 3 are stolen. How many shields does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain America started with 25 shields
    shields_initial = 25
    #He used 5 in the first mission
    shields_used_first_mission = 5
    #He used 4 in the second mission
    shields_used_second_mission = 4
    #2 of the shields are damaged
    shields_damaged = 2
    #3 of the shields are stolen
    shields_stolen = 3
    #The answer is
    result = shields_initial - shields_used_first_mission - shields_used_second_mission - shields_damaged - shields_stolen
    return result

    cookies_initial = 1000
    #She ate 100 of them

    #She then ate 10% of the remaining

    total_cheerleaders = 22
    #Number of senior cheerleaders
    seniors = 5

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel has 1000 superpowers. 300 of them are energy powers. 400 of them are strength powers. 200 of them are flight powers. The rest are superpowers that can only be described as "magic". How many superpowers does Captain Marvel have that can only be described as "magic"?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of superpowers
    total_superpowers = 1000
    #Number of energy, strength, and flight superpowers
    energy_superpowers = 300
    strength_superpowers = 400
    flight_superpowers = 200
    #Number of superpowers that can only be described as "magic"
    magic_superpowers = total_superpowers - energy_superpowers - strength_superpowers - flight_superpowers
    return magic_superpowers
Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question: A train leaves New York at 10:00 am traveling at 100 miles per hour. 
A second train leaves Boston at 11:00 am traveling at 150 miles per hour. 
New York and Boston are 200 miles apart. 
When do the trains pass each other?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A train leaves New York at 10:00 am traveling at 100 miles per hour
    train_1_time = 10
    train_1_speed = 100
    #A second train leaves Boston at 11:00 am traveling at 150 miles per hour
    train_2_time = 11
    train_2_speed = 150
    #New York and Boston are 200 miles apart
    distance = 200
    #The answer is
    result = (train_1_speed * (train_2_time - train_1_time)) / (train_1_speed - train_2_speed)

    passengers = 500
    #100 of them are in the first class cabin
    first_class = 100
    #200 of them are in the business class cabin
    business_class = 200
    #The rest of the passengers are in the economy class cabin. The answer is

Topic: cars ### Response: 
Question: A 4-lane highway has 3,000 cars per lane. A 2-lane highway has 2,000 cars per lane. How many more cars are on the 4-lane highway than the 2-lane highway?
Solution:
def solution():
    #4-lane highway has 3,000 cars per lane
    four_lane_cars_per_lane = 3000
    #2-lane highway has 2,000 cars per lane
    two_lane_cars_per_lane = 2000
    #4-lane highway has 4 lanes
    four_lane_lanes = 4
    #2-lane highway has 2 lanes
    two_lane_lanes = 2
    #The answer is
    result = (four_lane_cars_per_lane * four_lane_lanes) - (two_lane_cars_per_lane * two_lane_lanes)
    return result

Topic: lacrosse ### Response: 
Question: A lacrosse team has 10 players. They all need to have 2 sticks, 1 helmet, and 1 pair of pads. How many total pieces of equipment do they need?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The team has 10 players
    players = 10
    #Each player needs 2 sticks, 1 helmet, and 1 pair of pads
    sticks_per_player = 2
    helmets_per_player = 1
    pads_per_player = 1
    #The total number of each item is
    total_sticks = players * sticks_per_player
    total_helmets = players * helmets_per_player
    total_pads = players * pads_per_player
    #The total number of pieces of equipment is
    total_equipment = total_sticks + total_helmets + total_pads
    return total_equipment

Topic: lacrosse ### Response: 
Question: A lacrosse team has 32 players. 10 of them are 1.83 m tall. 9 of them are 1.93 m tall. 8 of them are 2.03 m tall. 5 of them are 2.13 m tall. What is the average height of the team in meters?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The number of players
    players = 32
    #10 of them are 1.83 m tall
    tall_1 = 10
    #9 of them are 1.93 m tall
    tall_2 = 9
    #8 of them are 2.03 m tall
    tall_3 = 8
    #5 of them are 2.13 m tall
    tall_4 = 5
    #The answer is
    result = (tall_1 * 1.83 + tall_2 * 1.93 + tall_3 * 2.03 + tall_4 * 2.13) / players
    return result

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: The velociraptor population has 5000 dinosaurs. The population grows 5% per year. How many velociraptors are there after 10 years?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The velociraptor population has 5000 dinosaurs
    velociraptor_population = 5000
    #The population grows 5% per year
    population_growth = 0.05
    #There are 10 years
    num_years = 10
    #The population grows
    population_growth_per_year = population_growth * velociraptor_population
    #Per year. The answer is
    result = velociraptor_population + (population_growth_per_year * num_years)
    return result

    #Members from 9th and 10th grades
    members_9th_10th = total_members - members_11th_12th
    return members_9th_10th

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response:

Solution:
def solution():

    superpowers_initial = 1000
    #She uses 10 superpowers per day
    superpowers_per_day = 10
    #There are 7 days in a week
    num_days = 7
    #She used 10 superpowers per day for 7 days. The answer is
    result = superpowers_initial - superpowers_per_day * num_days
    return result

Topic: Captain America ### Response: 
Question: Captain America has 300 shields. 
He uses 15% of them on the Red Skull. 
He then uses 10% of the remaining on the Winter Soldier. 
How many shields does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain America started with 300 shields
    shields_initial = 300
    #He used 15% of them on the Red Skull
    shields_used_red_skull = 0.15 * shields_initial
    #He then used 10% of the remaining on the Winter Soldier
    shields_used_winter_soldier = 0.10 * (shields_initial - shields_used_red_skull)
    #The answer is
    result = shields_initial - shields_used_red_skull - shields_used_winter_soldier
    return result

Topic: candy ### Response:

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total candy
    total_candy = 100
    #Chocolate
    chocolate = total_candy * 0.2
    #Gummies
    gummies = total_candy * 0.15
    #Sour
    sour = total_candy * 0.1
    #Lollipops
    lollipops = total_candy * 0.05
    #Hard candy
    hard_candy = total_candy * 0.5
    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: A T-Rex is chasing a triceratops. The T-Rex is 200 feet away from the triceratops and is running at 50 feet per second. The triceratops is running at 30 feet per second. How far away will the triceratops be from the T-Rex in 10 seconds?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The T-Rex is 200 feet away from the triceratops
    distance_away = 200
    #The T-Rex is running at 50 feet per second
    t_rex_speed = 50
    #The triceratops is running at 30 feet per second
    triceratops_speed = 30
    #The answer is
    result = distance_away - (t_rex_speed - triceratops_speed) * 10
    return result

Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response: 
Question: Hello Kitty has 5000 Hello Kitty stickers. She uses 2000 Hello Kitty stickers to decorate her room. She then uses 1/4 of the remaining Hello Kitty stickers to decorate her car. How many Hello Kitty stickers does Hello Kitty have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Hello Kitty has 5000 Hello Kitty stickers
    stickers_initial = 5000
    #She uses 2000 Hello Kitty stickers to decorate her room
    stickers_used_room = 2000
    #She then uses 1/4 of the remaining Hello Kitty stickers to decorate her car
    stickers_used_car = (stickers_initial - stickers_used_room) * 1/4
    #The answer is
    result = stickers_initial - stickers_used_room - stickers_used_car
    return result

    #Barbie has 100 pairs of shoes
    shoes = 100
    #20 of the pairs of shoes are high heels
    high_heels = 20
    #15 of the pairs of shoes are sneakers
    sneakers = 15
    #25 of the pairs of shoes are sandals

    #40 of the pairs of shoes are boots
    boots = 40

Topic: pizza ### Response: 
Question: A pizzeria sells 12-slice pizzas. 100 pizzas were sold on Monday, 200 on Tuesday, and 300 on Wednesday. How many pizza slices were sold?

Solution:
def solution():
    #12-slice pizzas were sold
    slices_per_pizza = 12
    #100 pizzas were sold on Monday, 200 on Tuesday, and 300 on Wednesday
    pizzas_sold_monday = 100
    pizzas_sold_tuesday = 200
    pizzas_sold_wednesday = 300
    #The answer is
    result = (pizzas_sold_monday + pizzas_sold_tuesday + pizzas_sold_wednesday) * slices_per_pizza
    return result

Question: Batman can fly at 300 miles per hour. He can also run at 100 miles per hour. If he flies for 2 hours and runs for 3 hours, how many miles has he covered?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Batman can fly at 300 miles per hour
    batman_flight_speed = 300
    #He can run at 100 miles per hour
    batman_run_speed = 100
    #He flies for 2 hours
    flight_hours = 2
    #He runs for 3 hours
    run_hours = 3
    #The answer is
    result = (batman_flight_speed * flight_hours) + (batman_run_speed * run_hours)
    return result

Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 
Question: Serena Williams has 24 Grand Slam titles. She has 7 Australian Open titles, 3 French Open titles, 7 Wimbledon titles, and 6 US Open titles. How many Grand Slam titles has she won outside of Australia, France, and England?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams has 24 Grand Slam titles
    grand_slam_titles = 24
    #She has 7 Australian Open titles
    australian_open_titles = 7
    #3 French Open titles
    french_open_titles = 3
    #7 Wimbledon titles
    wimbledon_titles = 7
    #and 6 US Open titles
    us_open_titles = 6
    #The answer is
    result = grand_slam_titles - australian_open_titles - french_open_titles - wimbledon_titles - us_open_titles
    return result
Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Question: A Minecraft world has 2000000 blocks. 1000000 of the blocks are dirt, 1/10 of the dirt is turned into farmland, and 1/10 of the farmland is turned into a crop. How many blocks are the crop?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of blocks
    total_blocks = 2000000
    #Number of dirt blocks
    dirt_blocks = 1000000
    #Number of dirt blocks turned into farmland
    farmland_blocks = dirt_blocks / 10
    #Number of farmland blocks turned into a crop
    crop_blocks = farmland_blocks / 10
    #The answer is
    result = crop_blocks
    return result

Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 
Question: There are 100 cheerleaders in the squad. 30 of them are freshmen, 40 of them are sophomores, and 10 of them are both freshmen and sophomores. How many cheerleaders in the squad are juniors or seniors?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of cheerleaders
    total_cheerleaders = 100
    #Number of freshmen cheerleaders
    freshmen_cheerleaders = 30
    #Number of sophomore cheerleaders
    sophomore_cheerleaders = 40
    #Number of cheerleaders that are both freshmen and sophomores
    both_types = 10
    #Number of cheerleaders that are juniors or seniors is
    juniors_or_seniors = total_cheerleaders - (freshmen_cheerleaders + sophomore_cheerleaders - both_types)
    return juniors_or_seniors
Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response:  Question: Patrick Mahomes has thrown 50 touchdowns this year. 20 of them were thrown in the first half of the season, and 30 were thrown in the second half of the season. How many touchdowns did Patrick Mahomes throw in each quarter?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Patrick Mahomes has thrown 50 touchdowns this year
    total_touchdowns = 50
    #20 of them were thrown in the first half of the season, and 30 were thrown in the second half of the season
    first_half_touchdowns = 20
    second_half_touchdowns = 30
    #The answer is
    result = first_half_touchdowns / 2 + second_half_touchdowns / 2
    return result

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response:  Question: There are 100 dinosaurs in a forest. 10 of these dinosaurs are T-Rexes. 20 of these dinosaurs are velociraptors. 30 of these dinosaurs are brachiosauruses. 40 of these dinosaurs are stegosauruses. How many of the dinosaurs are not one of the four listed?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of dinosaurs
    total_dinosaurs = 100
    #Number of T-Rexes, velociraptors, brachiosauruses, and stegosauruses
    t_rex = 10
    velociraptor = 20
    brachiosaurus = 30
    stegosaurus = 40
    #The answer is
    result = total_dinosaurs - t_rex - velociraptor - brachiosaurus - stegosaurus
    return result
Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question: The express train from New York to Boston leaves at 9:00 a.m. and takes 3 hours to get to Boston. The local train leaves at 10:00 a.m. and takes 4 hours to get to Boston. What time does the local train arrive in Boston?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The express train leaves at 9:00 a.m.
    express_train_departure = 9
    #The express train takes 3 hours
    express_train_time = 3
    #The local train leaves at 10:00 a.m.
    local_train_departure = 10
    #The local train takes 4 hours
    local_train_time = 4
    #The answer is
    result = express_train_departure + express_train_time + local_train_departure + local_train_time
    return result
Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response: 
Question: Wonder Woman can lasso 25 bad guys in 10 minutes. 
How many bad guys can she lasso in 2 hours?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Wonder Woman can lasso 25 bad guys in 10 minutes
    bad_guys_10_minutes = 25
    #1 hour is 60 minutes
    minutes_in_1_hour = 60
    #2 hours is 120 minutes
    minutes_in_2_hours = 2 * 60
    #The answer is
    result = (bad_guys_10_minutes / 10) * (minutes_in_2_hours)
    return result

    #He used 1000 photon blasts in a battle
    photon_blasts_used = 1000

    return result

Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Iron Man has 100 suits. 20% of them are Mark I suits, 10% of them are Mark II suits, 20% of them are Mark III suits, and the rest are Mark IV suits. How many suits are Mark IV suits?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of suits
    total_suits = 100
    #Percentage of Mark I suits
    mark_i_suits_percent = 20
    #Percentage of Mark II suits
    mark_ii_suits_percent = 10
    #Percentage of Mark III suits
    mark_iii_suits_percent = 20
    #Mark IV suits are the rest
    mark_iv_suits_percent = 100 - mark_i_suits_percent - mark_ii_suits_percent - mark_iii_suits_percent
    #The answer is
    result = total_suits * mark_iv_suits_percent / 100
    return

Topic: unicorns ### Response: 
Question: There are 25 unicorns in a herd. 1/4 of the herd are white unicorns, 1/3 of the herd are black unicorns, and the rest are rainbow unicorns. How many rainbow unicorns are in the herd?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total unicorns in the herd
    total_unicorns = 25
    #1/4 of the herd are white unicorns
    white_unicorns = total_unicorns / 4
    #1/3 of the herd are black unicorns
    black_unicorns = total_unicorns / 3
    #The rest are rainbow unicorns
    rainbow_unicorns = total_unicorns - white_unicorns - black_unicorns
    #The answer is
    result = rainbow_unicorns
    return result

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 
Question: The stegosaurus is 30 feet long. The apatosaurus is 3 times as long as the stegosaurus. The brachiosaurus is 2 times as long as the apatosaurus. How long is the brachiosaurus?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The stegosaurus is 30 feet long
    stegosaurus_length = 30
    #The apatosaurus is 3 times as long as the stegosaurus
    apatosaurus_length = stegosaurus_length * 3
    #The brachiosaurus is 2 times as long as the apatosaurus
    brachiosaurus_length = apatosaurus_length * 2
    #The answer is
    result = brachiosaurus_length
    return result

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 
Question: A vanilla ice cream cone costs 3 dollars. A chocolate ice cream cone costs 4 dollars. 150 vanilla ice cream cones and 200 chocolate ice cream cones were sold. How much more did the chocolate ice cream cones make than the vanilla ice cream cones?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A vanilla ice cream cone costs 3 dollars
    vanilla_cost = 3
    #A chocolate ice cream cone costs 4 dollars
    chocolate_cost = 4
    #150 vanilla ice cream cones and 200 chocolate ice cream cones were sold
    vanilla_sold = 150
    chocolate_sold = 200
    #The answer is
    result = (chocolate_sold * chocolate_cost) - (vanilla_sold * vanilla_cost)
    return result

Topic: Harry Potter ### Response: 
Question: Harry Potter, Hermione Granger, and Ron Weasley are in a duel. Harry has 10 spells, Hermione has 14, and Ron has 20. If they each use 4 spells, how many spells do they have left?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Harry, Hermione, and Ron have 10, 14, and 20 spells, respectively
    harry_spells = 10
    hermione_spells = 14
    ron_spells = 20
    #They each use 4 spells
    spells_used = 4
    #The answer is
    harry_left = harry_spells - spells_used
    hermione_left = hermione_spells - spells_used
    ron_left = ron_spells - spells_used
    result = harry_left + hermione_left + ron_left
    return result

Topic: lacrosse ### Response:  Question: A lacrosse team has 12 players. 8 of the players are on the field, and the rest are on the sidelines. 3 of the players on the sidelines are goalies. How many non-goalie players are on the sidelines?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A lacrosse team has 12 players
    total_players = 12
    #8 of the players are on the field
    players_on_field = 8
    #The rest are on the sidelines
    players_on_sidelines = total_players - players_on_field
    #3 of the players on the sidelines are goalies
    goalies = 3
    #The answer is
    result = players_on_sidelines - goalies
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: In a volleyball match, the home team scored 3 points in the first set, 5 in the second set, and 7 in the third set. The away team scored 4 points in the first set, 6 in the second set, and 8 in the third set. How many more points did the away team score than the home team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Home team points
    home_points_set_1 = 3
    home_points_set_2 = 5
    home_points_set_3 = 7
    #Away team points
    away_points_set_1 = 4
    away_points_set_2 = 6
    away_points_set_3 = 8
    #The answer is
    result = (away_points_set_1 + away_points_set_2 + away_points_set_3) - (home_points_set_1 + home_points_set_2 + home_points_set_3)
    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: A field hockey team has 6 players. 3 of the players are 15 years old. 2 of the players are 16. 1 of the players is 14. How many years old is the average player on the team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Number of 15-year-old players
    players_15 = 3
    #Number of 16-year-old players
    players_16 = 2
    #Number of 14-year-old players
    players_14 = 1
    #Total number of players
    total_players = players_15 + players_16 + players_14
    #Total age of all players
    total_age = players_15 * 15 + players_16 * 16 + players_14 * 14
    #Average age of all players
    average_age = total_age / total_players
    return average_age

Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: 
Iron Man can fly 1000 feet per second. He has to fly to the moon, which is 238,900 miles away from Earth. How long will it take him to get there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man can fly 1000 feet per second
    feet_per_second = 1000
    #The moon is 238,900 miles away from Earth
    miles_to_moon = 238900
    #1 mile = 5280 feet
    feet_per_mile = 5280
    #The answer is
    result = miles_to_moon * feet_per_mile / feet_per_second
    return result

    #Total number of blocks
    total_blocks = 2000000
    #Number of dirt blocks
    dirt_blocks = 1000000
    #Number of dirt blocks turned into farmland
    farmland_blocks = dirt_blocks / 10
    #Number of farmland blocks turned into a crop
    crop_blocks = farmland_blocks / 10

    result = crop_blocks
    return result

Topic: swimming ### Response:  Question: 30 students are at the pool. 10 of the students are in the shallow end. 20 of the students are in the deep end. 25% of the students are swimming. How many students are swimming?
Solution:
def solution():
    #30 students are at the pool
    total_students = 30
    #10 of the students are in the shallow end
    shallow_students = 10
    #20 of the students are in the deep end
    deep_students = 20
    #25% of the students are swimming
    swimming_students_percentage = 0.25
    #The answer is
    result = (total_students - shallow_students - deep_students) * swimming_students_percentage
    return result

How many seconds can Captain Marvel fly and shoot energy blasts?

    energy_total = 1000
    #She can use 50 units of energy per second to fly
    energy_fly = 50
    #She can use 20 units of energy per second to shoot energy blasts

    #The answer is

Topic: cookies ### Response: 
Question: There are 100 cookies. 1/3 of the cookies are chocolate chip cookies. 1/2 of the remaining cookies are peanut butter cookies. How many cookies are not chocolate chip or peanut butter cookies?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of cookies
    total_cookies = 100
    #Number of chocolate chip cookies
    chocolate_chip_cookies = total_cookies * 1/3
    #Number of peanut butter cookies
    peanut_butter_cookies = (total_cookies - chocolate_chip_cookies) * 1/2
    #Number of cookies that are not chocolate chip or peanut butter cookies
    other_cookies = total_cookies - chocolate_chip_cookies - peanut_butter_cookies
    return other_cookies

Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Iron Man has 2250 gold bricks. He is building a fortress that requires 1200 gold bricks. He is also building a mansion that requires 3/4 as many gold bricks as the fortress. How many gold bricks does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man started with 2250 gold bricks
    gold_bricks_initial = 2250
    #The fortress requires 1200 gold bricks
    gold_bricks_fortress = 1200
    #The mansion requires 3/4 as many gold bricks as the fortress
    gold_bricks_mansion = (3/4) * gold_bricks_fortress
    #The answer is
    result = gold_bricks_initial - gold_bricks_fortress - gold_bricks_mansion
    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 
Question: In a field hockey match, the home team, USA, scored 30 goals. The away team, Canada, scored 25. 5 of Canada's goals were disallowed. How many more goals did USA score than Canada?
Solution:
def solution():
    #USA scored 30 goals
    usa_goals = 30
    #Canada scored 25 goals
    canada_goals = 25
    #5 of Canada's goals were disallowed
    canada_disallowed_goals = 5
    #Canada's disallowed goals don't count, so they actually scored
    canada_goals_actual = canada_goals - canada_disallowed_goals
    #The answer is
    result = usa_goals - canada_goals_actual
    return result

Topic: lacrosse ### Response: 
Question: A lacrosse team has 24 players. 11 of the players are from the United States. 7 of the players are from Canada. 4 of the players are from Australia. 2 of the players are from the United Kingdom. How many players are not from the United States, Canada, Australia, or the United Kingdom?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 24
    #Players from the US, Canada, Australia, and the UK
    players_us = 11
    players_canada = 7
    players_australia = 4
    players_uk = 2
    #Players not from the US, Canada, Australia, or the UK
    players_not_us_canada_australia_uk = total_players - (players_us + players_canada + players_australia + players_uk)
    return players_not_us_canada_australia_uk
Topic: trains ### Response: 
Question: A train is traveling at 100 miles per hour. It travels for 10 minutes. How far does it travel?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The train travels at 100 miles per hour
    miles_per_hour = 100
    #It travels for 10 minutes
    minutes = 10
    #1 hour is 60 minutes
    minutes_1_hour = 60
    #The answer is
    result = (miles_per_hour * minutes) / minutes_1_hour
    return result

Topic: swimming ### Response:  Question: A swimmer swims 1000 meters. 1/3 of them are breaststroke. 1/5 of them are butterfly. 1/8 of them are backstroke. How many meters of the race were freestyle?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total meters swam
    total_meters_swam = 1000
    #Meters swam breaststroke
    meters_breaststroke = (1/3) * total_meters_swam
    #Meters swam butterfly
    meters_butterfly = (1/5) * total_meters_swam
    #Meters swam backstroke
    meters_backstroke = (1/8) * total_meters_swam
    #The answer is
    result = total_meters_swam - meters_breaststroke - meters_butterfly - meters_backstroke
    return result
Topic: cookies ### Response: 
Question: I baked 120 chocolate chip cookies. I ate 1/5 of them. I then gave 2/5 of the remaining cookies to my friends. How many cookies do I have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #I baked 120 cookies
    cookies_baked = 120
    #I ate 1/5 of them
    cookies_eaten = cookies_baked / 5
    #I then gave 2/5 of the remaining cookies to my friends
    cookies_given = (cookies_baked - cookies_eaten) / 5
    #The answer is
    result = cookies_baked - cookies_eaten - cookies_given
    return result

Question: The Brazilian soccer team scored 10 goals. The Argentinian soccer team scored 5 fewer goals than the Brazilian team. The Argentinian team scored 1/4 as many goals as the Brazilian team. How many goals did the Argentinian team score?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The Brazilian soccer team scored 10 goals
    brazilian_goals = 10
    #The Argentinian soccer team scored 5 fewer goals than the Brazilian team
    argentine_goals = brazilian_goals - 5
    #The Argentinian team scored 1/4 as many goals as the Brazilian team
    argentine_goals_2 = brazilian_goals / 4
    #The answer is
    result = argentine_goals
    return result

Topic: basketball ### Response: 
Question: The Golden State Warriors have 3000 points. 50% of the points are from 3-pointers, 20% of the points are from free throws, and the rest are from 2-pointers. How many points are from 2-pointers?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The Golden State Warriors have 3000 points
    points = 3000
    #50% of the points are from 3-pointers
    three_pointers = points * 0.5
    #20% of the points are from free throws
    free_throws = points * 0.20
    #The rest are from 2-pointers
    two_pointers = points - three_pointers - free_throws
    #The answer is
    result = two_pointers
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response:  Question: The volleyball team has 12 players. 4 of the players are 15 years old, 3 are 16, 2 are 17, and the rest are 18. How many players are 18?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of players
    total_players = 12
    #Number of players of each age
    players_15 = 4
    players_16 = 3
    players_17 = 2
    #The answer is
    result = total_players - (players_15 + players_16 + players_17)
    return result

Topic: Spiderman ### Response: 
Question: Spiderman, the superhero, is 6 feet tall.  He wears shoes that are 1 inch thick.  How tall is he in inches?  (1 foot is 12 inches)
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman's height in feet
    spiderman_height_feet = 6
    #Spiderman's shoe thickness in inches
    shoe_thickness = 1
    #1 foot is 12 inches
    feet_to_inches = 12
    #Spiderman's height in inches is
    spiderman_height_inches = spiderman_height_feet * feet_to_inches + shoe_thickness
    return spiderman_height_inches

Topic: Fortnite ### Response: 
Question:

- 20 of the players are using a shotgun
- 30 of the players are using an assault rifle
- 20 of the players are using a sniper rifle
- 30 of the players are using a pistol

How many players are not using a shotgun, assault rifle, sniper rifle, or pistol?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The total number of players
    total_players = 100
    #The number of players using a shotgun, assault rifle, sniper rifle, or pistol
    shotgun = 20
    assault_rifle = 30
    sniper_rifle = 20
    pistol = 30
    #The answer is
    result = total_players - shotgun - assault_rifle - sniper_rifle - pistol
    return result

Topic: football ### Response: 
Question: Tom Brady has 4000 yards. He throws 200 yards in the first quarter, 400 yards in the second quarter, 300 yards in the third quarter, and 100 yards in the fourth quarter. How many yards does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Tom Brady has 4000 yards
    yards_initial = 4000
    #He throws 200 yards in the first quarter
    yards_first_quarter = 200
    #He throws 400 yards in the second quarter
    yards_second_quarter = 400
    #He throws 300 yards in the third quarter
    yards_third_quarter = 300
    #He throws 100 yards in the fourth quarter
    yards_fourth_quarter = 100
    #The answer is
    result = yards_initial - yards_first_quarter - yards_second_quarter - yards_third_quarter - yards_fourth_quarter

Topic: cats ### Response: 
Question: There are 5 cats in a house. 3 of the cats are 2 years old. 1 of the cats is 4 years old. 1 of the cats is 6 years old. How many years old are the cats in the house?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Number of cats that are 2 years old
    cats_2_years_old = 3
    #Number of cats that are 4 years old
    cats_4_years_old = 1
    #Number of cats that are 6 years old
    cats_6_years_old = 1
    #The answer is
    result = cats_2_years_old * 2 + cats_4_years_old * 4 + cats_6_years_old * 6
    return result

Topic: soccer ### Response: 
Question: 12000 people in a stadium are watching a soccer game. 20% of the people are wearing red. 30% of the people are wearing blue. 25% of the people are wearing yellow. 15% of the people are wearing green. 10% of the people are wearing other colors. How many people are wearing other colors?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of people
    total_people = 12000
    #Percentage of people wearing red, blue, yellow, and green
    red_percent = 0.20
    blue_percent = 0.30
    yellow_percent = 0.25
    green_percent = 0.15
    #Percentage of people wearing other colors
    other_colors_percent = 0.10
    #The answer is
    result = total_people * other_colors_percent
    return result

    distance = 200
    #The answer is
    result = distance / speed_reduced
    return result

Topic: trains ### Response:  Question: A train leaves Chicago at 10:00am and arrives in Denver at 10:00pm. The train travels at an average speed of 50 miles per hour. How far is it from Chicago to Denver?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A train leaves Chicago at 10:00am and arrives in Denver at 10:00pm
    train_departure_time = 10
    train_arrival_time = 10
    #The train travels at an average speed of 50 miles per hour
    train_speed = 50
    #The answer is
    result = (train_arrival_time - train_departure_time) * train_speed
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response: 
Question: A car is traveling 220 miles. It has to travel 20% of the way in the rain, 30% of the way in the snow, and 50% of the way in the sunshine. How many miles does it travel in the sunshine?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The car is traveling 220 miles
    total_miles = 220
    #20% of the way is in the rain
    rain_miles = 0.2 * total_miles
    #30% of the way is in the snow
    snow_miles = 0.3 * total_miles
    #50% of the way is in the sunshine
    sunshine_miles = 0.5 * total_miles
    #The answer is
    result = sunshine_miles
    return result

Topic: Iron Man ### Response: 
Question: Iron Man has 1000 missiles. He uses 1/5 of them to fight the Mandarin. He then uses 2/3 of what is left to fight the Ten Rings. How many missiles does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man started with 1000 missiles
    missiles_initial = 1000
    #He used 1/5 of them to fight the Mandarin
    missiles_used_mandarin = 1/5 * missiles_initial
    #He used 2/3 of what is left to fight the Ten Rings
    missiles_used_ten_rings = 2/3 * (missiles_initial - missiles_used_mandarin)
    #The answer is
    result = missiles_initial - missiles_used_mandarin - missiles_used_ten_rings
    return result

    coins = 100
    #He can buy 1 fire flower for 5 coins, 1 mushroom for 10 coins, and 1 star for 20 coins
    fire_flower_cost = 5
    mushroom_cost = 10
    star_cost = 20
    #The answer is
    fire_flowers = coins / fire_flower_cost
    mushrooms = coins / mushroom_cost

    return fire_flowers, mushrooms, stars

    #Each tribe has 15 clans
    clans_per_tribe = 15
    #The answer is
    result = provinces * tribes_per_province * clans_per_tribe
    return result
Topic: Superman ### Response:  Question: Superman can fly 200 miles per hour. He flew 300 miles in the morning and 200 miles in the afternoon. How many miles did he fly in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can fly 200 miles per hour
    superman_speed = 200
    #He flew 300 miles in the morning
    superman_miles_morning = 300
    #He flew 200 miles in the afternoon
    superman_miles_afternoon = 200
    #The answer is
    result = superman_speed * (superman_miles_morning + superman_miles_afternoon)
    return result

Topic: Superman ### Response: 
Question: Superman has 1000 superpowers. He uses 200 of them to fly, 300 of them to see through walls, and the rest of them to lift heavy objects. How many superpowers does he use to lift heavy objects?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman has 1000 superpowers
    superpowers = 1000
    #He uses 200 of them to fly
    superpowers_fly = 200
    #He uses 300 of them to see through walls
    superpowers_see_through_walls = 300
    #He uses the rest of them to lift heavy objects
    superpowers_lift_heavy_objects = superpowers - superpowers_fly - superpowers_see_through_walls
    return superpowers_lift_heavy_objects

    #12 of them are in the first half

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 
Question: 1000 people attended the volleyball tournament. 25% of the attendees were from the United States. 30% of the attendees were from the United Kingdom. 15% of the attendees were from the European Union. 10% of the attendees were from Australia. 20% of the attendees were from the rest of the world. How many attendees were from the United States?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total attendees
    total_attendees = 12000
    #Percentage of attendees from US, UK, EU, Australia and rest of the world
    us_percentage = 0.25
    uk_percentage = 0.30
    eu_percentage = 0.15
    au_percentage = 0.10
    rotw_percentage = 0.20
    #The answer is
    result = total_attendees * us_percentage
    return result
Topic: soccer ### Response: 
Question: 5000 people are in the stands at a football game. 750 of them are wearing the home team's jersey. 2500 are wearing the away team's jersey. The rest are wearing neutral jerseys. How many people are wearing neutral jerseys?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of people in the stands
    total_people = 5000
    #Number of people wearing home team's jersey
    home_team_jersey = 750
    #Number of people wearing away team's jersey
    away_team_jersey = 2500
    #Number of people wearing neutral jerseys is
    neutral_jersey = total_people - home_team_jersey - away_team_jersey
    return neutral_jersey

Topic: Iron Man ### Response:  Question: Iron Man has 5000 missiles. He uses 1000 missiles to destroy a building. He then uses 1/5 of the remaining missiles to destroy a tank. How many missiles does Iron Man have left?

    #Iron Man started with 5000 missiles
    missiles_initial = 5000
    #He used 1000 missiles to destroy a building
    missiles_used_building = 1000
    #He used 1/5 of the remaining missiles to destroy a tank
    missiles_used_tank = (missiles_initial - missiles_used_building) * 1/5
    #The answer is
    result = missiles_initial - missiles_used_building - missiles_used_tank
    return result

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response: 
Question: Captain Marvel is in a space battle. She has 3200 shields. Each blast from her ship uses 100 shields. She fires 15 blasts. How many shields does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel started with 3200 shields
    shields_initial = 3200
    #Each blast uses 100 shields
    shields_per_blast = 100
    #She fired 15 blasts
    blasts = 15
    #15 blasts at 100 shields a blast cost
    shields_spent = shields_per_blast * blasts
    #The answer is
    result = shields_initial - shields_spent
    return result
Topic: cookies ### Response: 
Question: A cookie factory produces 1000 cookies per day. 1/3 of the cookies are chocolate chip, 1/4 of the cookies are peanut butter, and the rest are oatmeal raisin. How many oatmeal raisin cookies does the factory produce each day?

Solution:
def solution():
    #A cookie factory produces 1000 cookies per day
    total_cookies_per_day = 1000
    #1/3 of the cookies are chocolate chip
    chocolate_chip_cookies = total_cookies_per_day / 3
    #1/4 of the cookies are peanut butter
    peanut_butter_cookies = total_cookies_per_day / 4
    #The answer is
    oatmeal_raisin_cookies = total_cookies_per_day - chocolate_chip_cookies - peanut_butter_cookies
    return oatmeal_raisin_cookies

    #She needs to fly 120 miles
    miles_to_fly = 120
    #The answer is
    result = miles_to_fly / miles_per_hour
    return result
Topic: planes ### Response: 
Question: 20 planes are at an airport. 10 more planes land at the airport. 5 of the planes that were at the airport when the 10 planes landed, take off. 2 of the planes that just landed, take off. How many planes are at the airport now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #20 planes are at an airport
    planes_initial = 20
    #10 more planes land at the airport
    planes_landed = 10
    #5 of the planes that were at the airport when the 10 planes landed, take off
    planes_took_off_1 = 5
    #2 of the planes that just landed, take off
    planes_took_off_2 = 2
    #The answer is
    result = planes_initial + planes_landed - planes_took_off_1 - planes_took_off_2
    return result
